# Praxis 2.0 ‚Äî Deep-Dive Audit (read-only)

_Lead-engineer audit of the full Praxis codebase. Generated 2026-06-26 via a multi-agent read-only sweep (foundation passes -> per-surface + focus deep-reads -> adversarial verification of every finding -> synthesis). No source was modified._

Ledger totals: **2 CRITICAL ¬∑ 19 HIGH ¬∑ 60 MEDIUM ¬∑ 49 LOW** (130 verified findings). COULD items: 144. Requires-live-verification: 128.

---

Praxis 2.0 is a mature, disciplined vanilla-JS codebase: ES3 conformance is effectively clean (zero `const`/`let`/arrow/`class`/template-literal violations across `js/` except two harness-exempt `.catch`/`.finally` files), CSS token discipline is strong (2900 `var()` uses, zero live hardcoded hex in `components.css`), and the architecture has real load-bearing patterns ‚Äî a single Yumi context source, a frozen fail-closed gate, and a documented Firestore merge-boundary chokepoint. The code's central weakness is **durability and data integrity**: cloud-save failures are silent and unrecoverable for everything except books, Artifacts never reach the cloud at all, and the merge-boundary backfill pattern is honored for only two of five record types ‚Äî so a device switch can silently lose user-authored arcs, journal entries, sub-theories, and themes. The secondary themes are a broad **WCAG contrast deficit** (the dominant meta ink, plus river/teal/journal/danger/wordmark, all fail AA on at least one ground), **canon-vs-IS drift** where mobile and declutter rules target classes the renderer no longer emits (so they silently no-op), and **~1,200+ LOC of dead code** carried in load-bearing files. Several flagship flows ‚Äî sub-theory publish, the intellectual register read view, and Yumi-in-margin on the writing page ‚Äî are structurally unimplemented.

## Top 10 findings by severity
1. **[CRITICAL] Silent unrecoverable cloud-save loss for arcs/notebook/subTheories/themes** ‚Äî js/state.js:2196-2279 ‚Äî each block clears its dirty flag then only `console.warn`s on failure (no re-dirty, no pending-guard like books have), so a transient write failure is permanent and the REPLACE-on-auth merge clobbers the local write on the next device, vanishing user-authored arcs, journal/marginalia, published sub-theories, and manual themes.
2. **[CRITICAL] Book Artifacts are localStorage-only, never synced to Firestore** ‚Äî js/views.js:10242 ‚Äî the ceremonial write-once "yours" object whose card copy promises permanence never reaches the cloud, so a new device, fresh install, or localStorage clear silently loses every Artifact.
3. **[HIGH] saveState() success bool is ignored by all 52 callers** ‚Äî js/state.js:2152 ‚Äî `sv()` swallows exceptions and returns false, so on quota-exceeded or private-mode browsers every save is a silent no-op with no user-visible error and in-memory state diverges from the "durable" store the file's own comment guarantees.
4. **[HIGH] All 5 proxies fail OPEN when PRAXIS_CLIENT_KEY is unset** ‚Äî netlify/functions/claude-proxy.js:22-35 ‚Äî the key check runs only inside `if (expectedKey){...}`, so a missing/mistyped env var turns the entire AI backend into an open relay forwarding anonymous POSTs to Anthropic/ElevenLabs/Google Books on billable keys (duplicated verbatim across all five functions).
5. **[HIGH] Primary chat path (sendMessage) has no fetch timeout or AbortController** ‚Äî js/yumi-brain.js:770 ‚Äî a proxy that accepts but never responds leaves the promise unsettled, so `.finally` never fires, `yumi_request_in_flight` stays true, and the chat locks (button disabled, typing indicator stuck) until a full reload ‚Äî the one interactive proxy call not wrapped in `_yumiWithTimeout`.
6. **[HIGH] renderArcDetail List branch reads arc.entryIds/bookIds.length unguarded** ‚Äî js/views.js:9924 ‚Äî an arc record lacking `entryIds` (the Firestore arc merge has no `ensureArcFields` backfill and never runs migrate) throws a TypeError and aborts the entire arc-detail render ‚Äî the same defensive-gap class as the v3.143 account white-screen.
7. **[HIGH] Sub-theory publish/register transition is unimplemented ‚Äî no theory can ever be published** ‚Äî js/views.js:7720-7745 ‚Äî `status` is only ever written `'draft'`, `publishedAt` is never assigned in any path, and the "Published" button only renders a transient read-only preview keyed by a mode arg; nothing reads `st.status`, so the central artifact has no terminal public state.
8. **[HIGH] --ink-3/--ink-4 meta text fails AA on every bright surface (3.41-3.56:1)** ‚Äî assets/components.css:2685-2691 ‚Äî the dominant meta/byline color (used as `color` 223+66 times) lands sub-AA on `--page`/`--surface` for small text like `.book-detail-meta` (11px) and `.notebook-entry-ts` (10px), so dates and bylines across book-detail, notebook, sub-theory, and about are unreadable for low-vision readers.
9. **[HIGH] Arcs grid never collapses to 1-up on mobile (canon F broken)** ‚Äî assets/components.css:5730-5733 ‚Äî the mobile-collapse override targets `.arcs-yours`/`.arcs-examples` as classes but the renderer emits those names as ids, so the base `repeat(3,1fr)` rule (no `minmax(0,‚Ä¶)`, no max-width guard) keeps three ~98px cards per row at 390px, wrapping/overflowing text and forcing horizontal page overflow.
10. **[HIGH] Long marginalia is clipped at 15em with no read-more, expand, or detail route** ‚Äî assets/components.css:10615 ‚Äî a hard `overflow:hidden` with no affordance makes the tail of a long note permanently unreachable; there is no `#entry/` route and no whole-card click, so the reader cannot finish reading their own writing ‚Äî failing the focus area's core job.

---

Largest: `js/views.js` 14,526; `js/state.js` 2,944; `js/yumi-brain.js` 2,800; `js/integrations.js` 2,073; `js/yumi-ui.js` 1,928; `js/arc-constellation.js` 1,849; `js/import-capture.js` 1,421; `js/writing-canvas.js` 659; `js/spotlight.js` 457; `js/tradition-forms-arc.js` 383; `js/voice-input.js` 167; `js/app.js` 56; `js/arcs.js` 12; `js/verify-engine.js` 11.

- **Load-order note:** `index.html` script order (state ‚Üí tradition-forms-arc ‚Üí arc-constellation ‚Üí integrations ‚Üí yumi-brain ‚Üí arcs ‚Üí voice-input ‚Üí yumi-ui ‚Üí spotlight ‚Üí writing-canvas ‚Üí views ‚Üí import-capture ‚Üí app) DIFFERS from the order documented in CLAUDE.md, and adds spotlight/writing-canvas/import-capture not listed there. `js/verify-engine.js` (11 LOC) is NOT referenced by index.html and NOT in the sw.js precache list.
- **CACHE_VERSION:** `praxis-v3.150` (sw.js:10).
- **Migration chain:** `SCHEMA_VERSION` default literal is `'1.9.3'` (state.js:272 / :1542) while the `migrate()` chain runs forward to `'1.26.0'` (~state.js:2939). Confirmed deliberate (the comment at ~state.js:2107-2113 explains a brand-new user must walk every migration step from the default anchor), not stale.

## PASS 1 ‚Äî Architecture & inventory (the IS map)

### Route / surface map

All routing is hash-based via `renderRoute()` (js/views.js:343). Dual-ground is set on `<body data-ground>` keyed off the raw hash head (js/views.js:369-371): dark = home/books/arcs/arc/account; bright = everything else.

| Route (hash) | Entry point | Ground |
|---|---|---|
| `#home` | `renderHome()` views.js:606 | dark |
| `#books` | `renderShelf()` views.js:2522 | dark |
| `#arcs` | `renderArcsPage()` views.js:2244 | dark |
| `#arc/<id>` | `renderArcDetail()` views.js:9477 | dark |
| `#arc/<id>/new-subtheory` | `createSubTheory()` ‚Üí redirect, views.js:482 | (transient) |
| `#subtheory/<id>` | `renderSubTheoryPage()` views.js:7467 | bright |
| `#book/<id>` | `renderBookDetail()` views.js:5963 | bright |
| `#artifact/<id>` | `renderArtifact()` views.js:8538 | bright |
| `#account` | `renderAccountPage()` views.js:13167 | dark |
| `#about` | `renderAbout()` views.js:14222 | bright |
| `#yumi-sees` | `renderWhatYumiSeesPage()` views.js:11303 | bright (reached from Yumi panel, not nav) |
| _(empty / unknown / `#notebook`)_ | `renderNotebook()` views.js:734 | bright (catch-all) |

Top-nav links (index.html:24-34): Home, Shelf (`#books`), Arcs, Notebook, About, Account. There is no explicit `#notebook` case in `renderRoute` ‚Äî the Notebook surface is the catch-all fallthrough for empty/unknown hashes.



## state.js ‚Äî state shape, storage, durability, migrations

`js/state.js` (2944 lines, HEAD `4f7e1b8`) owns the three storage primitives every other module routes through: the `ls()`/`sv()` localStorage wrappers, the live `state` object, and the `loadState`/`saveState`/`migrate` trio. It is the single most durability-critical file in the app. The headline finding is an **asymmetric cloud-durability model**: the books collection is hardened against transient Firestore failures (re-dirty-on-failure + a persisted pending-sync guard), but the other four synced collections (arcs, notebook entries, sub-theories, themes) have **neither** ‚Äî a failed cloud write is logged and forgotten, and the REPLACE-on-auth merge on the next device then deletes the local copy and splats the stale remote, silently losing the write.

### 1. State shape (verified)

The top-level `state` object is declared at `js/state.js:271-285`:

| Field | Kind | Keyed by | Line |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SCHEMA_VERSION` | string semver, default `'1.9.3'` | ‚Äî | :272 |
| `currentBookId` / `currentArcId` / `currentSubTheoryId` | scalar id-ref or null (open-pointers) | ‚Äî | :273-275 |
| `users` | per-user map: `{ yumiMemory, registerDefaults, profile, readerModel }` | uid | :276, shape seeded at :1020-1121 (`ensureUser`) |
| `books` | global user-agnostic catalog | bookId | :277 |
| `userBooks` | personal shelf `{ bookIds:[] }` | uid | :278 |
| `notebooks` | (legacy, effectively unused) | ‚Äî | :279 |
| `notebookEntries` | atomic writing unit (register/isPrivate/filed/images/bookIds/arcIds) | entryId | :280 |
| `bookArtifacts` | per user+book synthesis | `artifactKey(uid,bookId)` | :281 |
| `arcs` | reading threads (`bookIds`/`entryIds` as `{id,addedAt}`) | arcId | :282 |
| `subTheories` | published theory units (evidence/citationPins/x,y) | subTheoryId | :283 |
| `userThemes` | manual theme overlay | themeId | :284 |
| `seeds` | seed-idempotency markers (created lazily by migrate) | ‚Äî | :2534 |

The per-user record shape is authoritative in `ensureUser` (:1020-1121); `profile` carries 10 fields (`displayNameOverride, penName, onboardingSeen, tagline, yumiReadsAlong, yumiReaderModel, yumiWebGrounding, voiceOn, talkMode, values`).

### 2. localStorage is fully encapsulated (clean)

`ls()` (:252-260) and `sv()` (:262-269) are the **only** localStorage access in the entire `js/` tree. A scoped grep for the real API surface (`localStorage.getItem|setItem|removeItem|clear|key`) matched exactly two lines ‚Äî :254 and :264, both inside the wrappers ‚Äî and `sessionStorage` matched nothing. There is no raw `localStorage.*` call anywhere in views.js, integrations.js, or any other module. This invariant is solid.

### 3. Durability model + swallowed-failure sites

`saveState()` (:2147-2281) does one **synchronous** localStorage write (`var ok = sv(stateKey(), state)`, :2152) ‚Äî "the durability guarantee" per its own comment ‚Äî then fires up to five **fire-and-forget** per-collection Firestore writes gated on dirty flags. Three problems, in descending severity:

- **Cloud-write failure is silent and unretried for 4 of 5 collections (CRITICAL).** In each of the arcs/notebook/subTheories/themes blocks the dirty flag is cleared at the top of the block (`arcsDirty = false`, :2197; `notebookDirty = false`, :2218; `subTheoriesDirty = false`, :2239; `themesDirty = false`, :2260) and the failure branch is `console.warn` only ‚Äî it never re-sets the flag. Only the books block re-dirties on failure (`booksDirty = true`, :2191) AND is backed by the persisted `pendingBookSync` set (:785-831). The REPLACE-on-auth merge for arcs deletes every local arc for the uid before splatting remote (`integrations.js:133-149`); sub-theories (:169-178) and notebook follow the same REPLACE contract. So: edit an arc offline/under a transient 5xx ‚Üí localStorage OK, cloud write fails silently ‚Üí open another device ‚Üí stale remote REPLACE-deletes the edit. Books are immune to this exact path; arcs/notebook/subTheories/themes are not.
- **`saveState()`'s return value is never checked (HIGH).** `saveState` returns `ok` (the localStorage success bool), but 0 of the 52 `saveState()` call sites in views.js inspect it. `sv()` swallows any exception and returns `false` (:266-268), so on a quota-exceeded or private-mode device every save is a silent no-op with no user-visible signal and no console output ‚Äî the "durability guarantee" fails invisibly.
- **The only two try/catch blocks in the file** are in `ls`/`sv` (:257, :266); both swallow to a default / `false`. That is correct for `ls`, but `sv`'s swallow is the root of the silent-local-failure above.

The dirty-flag chokepoints themselves are well-factored: `markBooksDirty` (:764), `markArcsDirty` (:915), `markNotebookDirty` (:926), `markSubTheoriesDirty` (:936), `markThemesDirty` (:946), each consumed once in `saveState`.

### 4. Migration chain (1.0.0 ‚Üí 1.26.0)

`migrate()` (:2321-2942) is a clean forward-only `if (SCHEMA_VERSION === 'X') {...; = 'Y'}` ladder with an unknown-version pass-through (:2319 comment; future versions fall through untouched). Walked end-to-end, every step is either additive-with-type-guard (idempotent) or a deliberate version-stamp no-op (`1.1.0‚Üí1.2.0` :2331, `1.4.0‚Üí1.5.0` :2362, `1.9.2‚Üí1.9.3` :2496). The seed step `1.9.3‚Üí1.10.0` (:2503-2623) is double-guarded (version stamp + `seeds.pedagogyOfDesire.attempted`). Schema-field backfills onto `state.books` are correctly delegated to the documented `ensureBookFieldsAll` chokepoint at `1.10.0‚Üí1.11.0` (:2632), `1.19.0‚Üí1.20.0` (:2812), and `1.25.0‚Üí1.26.0` (:2937) ‚Äî and the Firestore merge path honors the same chokepoint (`integrations.js:601`), so the documented Firestore-bypass risk is closed for books.

The **default literal `'1.9.3'`** is a deliberate anchor, not stale: the comment at :2107-2114 ("Do NOT bump this default literal‚Ä¶ The chain does the work; the default literal stays the anchor") explains a brand-new user starts at 1.9.3 so cold-open `loadState` (:2135) walks the seed ladder. The same literal is re-asserted in `clearUserState()` (:1542). Two real residuals:
- `clearUserState()` (:1530-1543) wipes 10 maps but **omits `state.userThemes`** (a real map in the default object at :284) ‚Äî stale manual themes from a prior user survive an in-memory wipe.
- `migrate` uses `Array.isArray` 13√ó (e.g. :641, :2716) ‚Äî ES5, which the project's cscript JScript ES3 harness cannot evaluate. This is harmless at runtime (browsers only) but contradicts the CLAUDE.md claim that state.js is the harness-parseable promise-free file; the harness silently can't fully validate this file.

### 5. IndexedDB (photo blobs) ‚Äî error handling is correct

IndexedDB is used only for device-local notebook-photo blobs (refs-only stored in `state.notebookEntries[*].images`, migrate `1.20.0‚Üí1.21.0` :2822-2830). The access helpers live in views.js (`nbPhotoIdbOpen/Put/Get`, :1393-1434): each has a `window.indexedDB` feature-guard (:1394), try/catch around `.open`/`.transaction` (:1396-1398, :1412), and wires `onerror`/`tx.onerror`/`pr.onerror` to an `onErr` callback. A missing blob (e.g. another device) degrades to a graceful label (:1473 comment) rather than crashing. This is the durability bright spot of the storage layer.

### 6. Other observations

- `exportWorkspace()` (:1500-1528), wired to the account "Export to JSON" button (`views.js:14146`), **omits `bookArtifacts` and `userThemes`** ‚Äî a user backup silently loses their book syntheses and manual themes.
- Id generators (`genBookId` :981, `genArcId` :988, `genSubTheoryId` :996) use `Date.now()+'_'+Math.floor(Math.random()*1e6)`; the seed loop mints 5 ids in one tick but the 10^6 random space makes collision negligible ‚Äî not a finding.
- The `notebooks` map (:279) is declared but appears vestigial (schema 1.6.0 dropped `notebookId`); low-priority dead weight.

## Netlify Functions + Service Worker Audit

Scope: the five serverless proxies (`netlify/functions/claude-proxy.js` 70 LOC, `elevenlabs-proxy.js` 122, `google-books-proxy.js` 109, `transcribe-proxy.js` 162, `vision-proxy.js` 235), `sw.js` (133), and the SW registration block in `index.html` (lines 57-130). LOC via `wc -l`. No `netlify.toml`, `_headers`, or `_redirects` exist at repo root (`ls` returned "No such file"); the only config files are `firebase.json` (Firestore rules pointer) and `manifest.json`.

### 1. x-praxis-key gate ‚Äî enforced, but fail-OPEN by design

All five functions share a byte-identical gate block. The reject path is real and returns `401 {"error":"unauthorized"}` on a header mismatch:

- `claude-proxy.js:22-35` ‚Äî `var expectedKey = process.env.PRAXIS_CLIENT_KEY; if (expectedKey) { ‚Ä¶ if (providedKey !== expectedKey) return 401 }`
- `elevenlabs-proxy.js:40-53`, `google-books-proxy.js:22-35`, `transcribe-proxy.js:47-60`, `vision-proxy.js:22-35` ‚Äî same block, same line shape.

The gate reads both casings (`x-praxis-key` / `X-Praxis-Key`) and compares with `!==`. The client wires the matching header at every call site (`yumi-brain.js:94/770/926/‚Ä¶`, `views.js:5875`, `integrations.js:1449/1528/1863/2057`, `import-capture.js:143/1051`).

**The load-bearing weakness is structural:** the check runs only inside `if (expectedKey)`. When `PRAXIS_CLIENT_KEY` is unset or empty, the gate is skipped entirely and any anonymous POST is forwarded to the billable upstream (Anthropic / ElevenLabs / Google Books). A missing or mistyped env var silently converts the AI backend into an open relay. Memory records that the SEC header shipped "INERT until Preston sets the Netlify env var," i.e. there has been a live window with the gate off ‚Äî whether it is currently set is **[requires live verification]**. This is logged HIGH because the failure is silent and the cost is real (billable API spend + abuse surface).

### 2. Secret scan ‚Äî clean for upstream keys; shared secret is in the client

A scan for `sk-‚Ä¶`, `Bearer ‚Ä¶`, and `api[_-]?key:"‚Ä¶"` literals across `netlify/functions/` and `js/` returned **zero matches**. Every upstream credential is read from `process.env`:

- `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` (claude-proxy.js:46, vision-proxy.js:132)
- `ELEVENLABS_API_KEY` (elevenlabs-proxy.js:79, transcribe-proxy.js:120 ‚Äî same account key for TTS + STT)
- `GOOGLE_BOOKS_API_KEY` (google-books-proxy.js:59, optional)

Control: the same `grep -rn process.env` matched all of the above, proving the search is wired. Two values that *look* like secrets but are not upstream credentials: the **Firebase web config `apiKey`** at `integrations.js:21` (a public client identifier, correct to ship) and the **`PRAXIS_CLIENT_KEY`** 64-hex literal at `integrations.js:18`. The latter is the gate's own shared secret, shipped in the public bundle ‚Äî so the gate is anti-scraping friction, not authentication (anyone can lift it from DevTools). Logged MEDIUM with a COULD to move to server-side Firebase-ID-token verification.

### 3. CORS ‚Äî consistent wildcard, no credentialed-CORS bug

Every function emits `Access-Control-Allow-Origin: '*'` on every branch (OPTIONS, 401, 4xx, 5xx, success). `grep -rc Access-Control-Allow-Origin` counts 4/6/6/7/8 across the five files. A scan for `Allow-Credentials` returned **no matches** ‚Äî so the dangerous `*` + credentials pairing does **not** exist. Allowed methods (`POST, OPTIONS`) and allowed headers (`Content-Type, x-praxis-key`) are identical across all five preflight responses. This is safe as-is; tightening `*` to the known origin is a defense-in-depth COULD, not a defect.

### 4. Service worker ‚Äî cache-first shell, network pass-through for API; one precache gap is correct

`CACHE_VERSION = 'praxis-v3.150'` (sw.js:10). Strategy:

- **App shell (`APP_SHELL`, sw.js:12-33):** cache-first (`caches.match` ‚Üí cached, else network with `cache.put` of 200/basic responses; `.catch` ‚Üí `503` Response). Install uses `precacheFresh` (sw.js:57-68) with a `?sw_v=` cache-buster and `{cache:'reload'}` to defeat the old-SW interception/poisoning pattern ‚Äî a well-reasoned fix.
- **API + third-party (`isApiRequest`, sw.js:35-43):** network pass-through, `return` *before* `respondWith` (sw.js:105) so Firestore Listen streams don't pin the active worker and stall waiting-worker promotion. Matches `/.netlify/functions/`, openlibrary, googleapis, gstatic, firebaseio, firebaseapp.
- **Non-GET:** ignored (sw.js:100).

**Precache vs `<script src>` parity:** index.html loads 12 app JS files (`index.html:43-55`) plus 3 Firebase CDN scripts (40-42, correctly network-only). The 12 local scripts all appear in `APP_SHELL`. The single discrepancy is **`js/verify-engine.js`**, which is in neither index.html nor the precache. This is **correct**: the file is a comment-only tombstone ("verify-engine.js ‚Äî REMOVED", verify-engine.js:1-12) retained only to avoid a 404 during the v1‚Üív2 rollover. At v3.150 it is dead weight (logged LOW).

**Stale-bundle risk + SKIP_WAITING flow:** invalidation rides entirely on the manually-bumped `CACHE_VERSION` ‚Äî CLAUDE.md flags this as a recurring hazard (every JS change after a bump needs its own bump). The update flow is sound: `install` no longer calls `skipWaiting()` unconditionally; a new SW parks in `waiting` until the page posts `SKIP_WAITING` (sw.js:129-133) after the user clicks Reload on the banner (index.html:84-90). `controllerchange` (index.html:105-110) guards with `hadController` + a `refreshing` latch so the first install doesn't reload, and `visibilitychange` triggers `reg.update()` on focus (index.html:122-124). Live promotion behavior is **[requires live verification]**.

### 5. Failure modes ‚Äî graceful upstream relay, but several client calls can hang

Per-proxy server-side handling is solid:
- **Bad input:** `vision-proxy.js:41-51` validates `mediaType` against an allowlist and strips a stray data-URL prefix (53-59); `transcribe-proxy.js:74-93` enforces a base64 size cap (`MAX_AUDIO_B64_CHARS` 7.5M ‚Üí 413) and tolerantly strips any data-URL prefix; `google-books-proxy.js:40-49` and `elevenlabs-proxy.js:57-67` reject empty `q`/`text` with 400.
- **Upstream 4xx/5xx:** passed through with the real status, not masked as 500 ‚Äî `elevenlabs-proxy.js:88-98` relays the upstream JSON error; `google-books-proxy.js:73-100` reads the body as text first and try-parses so a non-JSON 429 isn't converted to a 500; `transcribe-proxy.js:127-137` and `vision-proxy.js:143-153` pass the status and log detail server-side only (never the audio/key/error text to the client). `vision-proxy.js:214-222` returns an honest `502 extraction-parse-failed` rather than fabricating books.

The gap is **client-side timeouts.** The project has a `_yumiWithTimeout` helper (`yumi-brain.js:642-654`) used on 11 gate/grader/web/move calls, but the **user-facing chat** fetch (`yumi-brain.js:770-805`), `summarizeAndRoll` (`:92`), **TTS** (`integrations.js:2055`), **Google Books** (`integrations.js:1447`), and the **vision scan** fetch (`views.js:5873`) all issue a bare `fetch().then()` with no `AbortController` and no timeout wrap. A stalled upstream leaves these pending indefinitely ‚Äî most visibly the chat 'thinking' state, which has no recovery path. The shelf-scan has a generous 20s+ `ccWatchdog` (`views.js:3169`) but it guards the *categorize* callback, not the vision fetch. Logged MEDIUM (chat hang); the rest are COULDs. The proxies themselves also have no server-side `AbortController` on their upstream fetch (separate COULD).

## Yumi Brain, Yumi UI & Integrations ‚Äî Audit

Scope: `js/yumi-brain.js` (2800 LOC), `js/yumi-ui.js` (1928 LOC), `js/integrations.js` (2073 LOC, the documented ES5 exception). HEAD `4f7e1b8` (CACHE_VERSION praxis-v3.150). All findings are static; behaviors that need a running browser are flagged for live verification.

### 1. The frozen gate and the single context source

The **eval gate** ("frozen gate") is `gradeUtterance(candidateText, readerInput)` at `js/yumi-brain.js:707`, fed by `YUMI_GATE_SYSTEM` (`:549`), the three-layer Part-3 rubric (Fidelity / No-leakage / Stance-and-safe). It is genuinely **fail-closed**: every failure mode ‚Äî empty candidate (`:710`), over-budget (`:719`), parse-fail (`_yumiParseGateVerdict:669`, anything-not-explicit-PASS ‚Üí fail), timeout/error (`:748-751`) ‚Äî resolves `{pass:false}`, never rejects. It is memoized by djb2 hash (`_yumiGateCache:608`, only definitive verdicts cached so a transient error can retry), soft-capped per day (`YUMI_GATE_DAILY_CAP=200`), and hard-bounded by `_yumiWithTimeout` (`YUMI_GATE_TIMEOUT_MS=12000`). The memo-hit check (`:714`) precedes the budget spend (`:717`), so a repeated candidate never burns budget. This is solid, defensible architecture.

**`assembleContextData()` (`:178`) is confirmed the single source** for the two context consumers it was built to serve: `buildContext()` (the model-prose blob) calls it at `:411`, and `getContextSnapshot` is a literal alias ‚Äî `getContextSnapshot: assembleContextData` (`:2748`). Both UI consumers read the alias: `views.js:11108` and `views.js:11311` (transparency view) and `yumi-ui.js:1088` ("what Yumi sees" panel). No parallel context-prose path exists. The master consent gate (`yumiReadsAlong === false` ‚Üí `recentEntries`/`recentArtifacts` emptied, `:326-330`) and the per-entry `isPrivate` skip (`:218`) both live here.

**However, the privacy predicate is NOT centralized.** The `isPrivate` filter is independently re-implemented at **7 sites** in yumi-brain.js (`:218` entries, `:266` artifacts, `:386` counts, `:1690` single-note move, `:1901` scan, `:2251` arc-voice evidence). The moves layer (`considerMove`/`considerNotice`/`considerArcVoice`/`considerProfileRefresh`) does **not** route through `assembleContextData` ‚Äî each carries its own copy of `isPrivate === true`. The contract holds today, but a future change to what counts as "private" must be made in all 7 places or a private note leaks into a prompt; "single enforcement point" is true for chat-context only, not for the move generators.

### 2. The move set and network/LLM failure handling

The five moves are present and wired: **QUIET** (default), **DRAW-OUT** + **COMPLICATE** (single-note router `generateMove:1602` / `MOVE_GEN_SYSTEM:1478`), **NOTICE** + **NAME** (cross-note layer `considerNotice:2029` / `considerName:2062`). Plus **arc-voice** (`considerArcVoice:2351`, explicitly *not* one of the five), the **classify router** (`classifyUtterance:2639`), web-grounding (`considerWebAngle:1400`), lens generation (`generateLenses:917`), and profile refresh (`considerProfileRefresh:2496`).

**Timeout coverage is inconsistent.** Eight LLM calls are wrapped in `_yumiWithTimeout` (gate, move-router, scan, name, arc-voice, profile, web-distiller, classify-router) and all resolve-not-reject on timeout/error ‚Äî these cannot hang. But **three raw `fetch().then()` chains have NO timeout**:
- `sendMessage` (`:770`) ‚Äî **the primary chat path**. This is the one that matters: in `yumi-ui.js` the send handler sets `yumi_request_in_flight=true` + disables the button (`:1230-1231`) and relies on `.finally` (`:1254`) to clear them. If the proxy connection hangs without responding (no RST), the `fetch` promise never settles, `.finally` never fires, and **the chat is permanently locked** (button disabled, typing indicator stuck) with no recovery short of a page reload. `_yumiWithTimeout` would have bounded it.
- `summarizeAndRoll` (`:92`) ‚Äî a hung fetch stalls `appendTurn`'s `shiftLoop` (`:159`), so `recentTurns` grows past cap unbounded (memory-only, low impact).
- `generateLenses` (`:926`) ‚Äî a hung fetch leaves the lens panel in its loading state.

`_yumiWithTimeout` itself (`:642`) rejects on a `setTimeout` but **never aborts the underlying `fetch`** (no `AbortController` anywhere ‚Äî grep confirms only one `setTimeout` and zero `AbortController` in yumi-brain.js). So even the "bounded" calls leak the in-flight connection; UI/promise state recovers, the socket does not. Acceptable for recovery, worth noting under load.

**Acknowledged asymmetric-memory bug (`sendMessage`, `:755-757`, by the author's own comment):** `appendTurn('user', userText)` runs at `:758` *before* the proxy call. If the call fails OR the gate suppresses the reply (`:798-800`), the user turn persists in `recentTurns` with no matching assistant turn, and the next `buildContext` feeds Yumi a dangling user line. Documented as a deferred limitation, still live.

The fire-and-forget UI seams (`maybeDrawOut` `views.js:1811`, `requestArcVoice` `views.js:9379`) call `.then()` with **no failure arm**. This is safe *only* because the orchestrators are documented to always resolve; if either ever rejected, `requestArcVoice` would strand the trigger button disabled showing "‚Ä¶" forever. Latent fragility resting on an invariant.

### 3. Firestore sync ‚Äî the merge-bypasses-migrate hazard

The known hazard is **partially fixed, partially still open.** `onAuthStateChanged` (`integrations.js:36`) REPLACE-merges six remote docs; none call `migrate()`. Per-collection backfill status at the merge boundary:
- **Books** ‚Äî `mergeRemoteBookDoc` (`:526`) calls `ensureBookFieldsAll(state.books)` *after* the copy (`:601`). **Fixed.**
- **Sub-theories** ‚Äî `backfillSubTheoryUserId` + `ensureSubTheoryFieldsAll` (`:188-199`). **Fixed.**
- **Notebook entries** ‚Äî **ad-hoc only**: three inline defaults (`filed` `:282`, journal-`isPrivate` `:298`, `images` `:309`). There is **no `ensureNotebookEntryFields` helper at all** (grep: none) ‚Äî any *future* notebook field added to `migrate()` will silently miss synced records.
- **Profile** ‚Äî explicit field-by-field whitelist (`:340-377`) symmetric with the `.set()` write list. **Fixed** (and heavily commented as the gotcha).
- **Arcs** ‚Äî splat only (`:145-149`), **zero field backfill.**
- **Themes** ‚Äî splat only (`:234-238`), **zero field backfill.**

The code's own comment (`:191-199`) names "ensure*FieldsAll at the merge boundary ‚Ä¶ the standing pattern for every future schema field," but arcs, themes, and notebook do not follow it. No present-day crash (migrate adds no per-arc/per-theme record fields today, verified `state.js:2321-2438`), but the pattern is unevenly applied and the next schema field on arcs/themes/notebook will reintroduce the exact data-shape drift this pattern exists to prevent.

### 4. volumeToBook ‚Äî categories are now captured (memory note is STALE)

The prior belief that `volumeToBook` discards `volumeInfo.categories` is **false at HEAD.** `volumeToBook` (`integrations.js:1717`) captures `rawCategories: (vi && vi.categories instanceof Array) ? vi.categories : []` (`:1740`), and a full Stage-2 LLM batch classifier consumes it (`classifyBooksViaLLM:1846`, `buildClassifyPrompt:1803` emits the `[subjects: ‚Ä¶]` hint). Lineage-readiness for category data exists on the canonical add path. Caveat: the two *lightweight* metadata fetchers `fetchGoogleBooks` (`:1462`) and `fetchBookByTitle` (`:1541`) build their own record shapes and do **not** extract categories ‚Äî only `volumeToBook` (used by `resolveBook`, the primary add path) does.

### 5. Client x-praxis-key consistency

**Every** client‚Üíproxy fetch carries `x-praxis-key: PRAXIS_CLIENT_KEY`. Verified by cross-referencing all 18 proxy fetch sites against the header grep: yumi-brain.js (10 sites: `:92,730,770,926,1372,1616,1990,2012,2323,2476,2656` ‚Äî header at +2 each), integrations.js (`:1447,1526,1861,1885,2055`), views.js vision-proxy (`:5873`), import-capture.js (`:141,1051`). No proxy fetch omits the key. The two `openlibrary.org` calls (`integrations.js:1380,1400`) correctly omit it ‚Äî they are third-party, not our gated proxy. `PRAXIS_CLIENT_KEY` is a hardcoded literal at `integrations.js:18`; the proxy only enforces it when the Netlify env var is set (server-side, out of scope here).

### 6. ES3 convention drift (app-source `.catch`/`.finally`)

Project hard rule: app JS uses two-arg `.then`, no `.catch`/`.finally` (only `integrations.js` is exempt). Violated in two **non-exempt** files: `yumi-brain.js:26,123` (`.catch` in `loadYumiVoice`/`summarizeAndRoll`) and `yumi-ui.js:1249,1254` (`.catch` + `.finally` in the chat send handler). These match the CLAUDE.md note that the cscript harness "cannot parse files using `.catch`/`.finally`" ‚Äî i.e. the team knowingly works around the rule and verifies these files on live deploy. Functionally fine; it is convention/consistency debt, and it means these two files are silently harness-exempt.


---

## PASS 2 ‚Äî Code health & infrastructure

## App-source audit: ES3 conformance, dead weight, duplication (js/ excluding integrations.js)

Scope: all client JS under `js/` except the documented exception `js/integrations.js`. Repo at HEAD `4f7e1b8` (CACHE_VERSION `praxis-v3.150`), working tree clean. The 13 in-scope files total 27,213 LOC; `js/integrations.js` (2,073 LOC) is excluded.

### 1. ES3 syntax conformance ‚Äî CLEAN for const/let/arrow/class/template; two harness-fail files for `.catch`/`.finally`

The four "no new-JS syntax" rules hold across every in-scope file. Each banned-syntax grep returned only false positives (comments and string/regex literals), confirmed by reading every hit:

| Construct | Raw grep hits (in `js/`) | True violations | Where the hits actually are |
|---|---|---|---|
| `\bconst\b` | 2 | 0 | `state.js:246`, `views.js:200` ‚Äî both the "no const, let, arrow‚Ä¶" guard comment |
| `\blet\b` | 10 | 0 | comments + prose strings ("let Yumi read along", "never let retrieved text‚Ä¶") |
| `=>` | 1 | 0 | `views.js:8698` ‚Äî comment "null => the renderer falls back‚Ä¶" |
| `\bclass\b` | 212 | 0 | every hit is `setAttribute('class', ‚Ä¶)`, a `class="‚Ä¶"` SVG/HTML string, or a comment; the strict regex `class\s+[A-Z]\w*\s*\{` / `extends` returns **zero** |
| backtick `` ` `` | 16 | 0 | all inside `//` comments or the regex char-class `/^["'\`]+/` (`yumi-brain.js:1319`) |

Control greps prove ripgrep was wired: `\bvar\b` and `\bfunction\b` both match heavily (1,585 `function` tokens across in-scope files; 442 unique top-level `^function` names in the four big files alone). A stricter arrow regex (`\)\s*=>` and `\w\s*=>\s*[\{\(\w]`) also returned only the one comment. **No `const`, `let`, arrow, `class`, or template literal exists in app source.**

Beyond syntax, the team is also disciplined about ES5+/ES6+ *runtime methods*: `.includes(`, `.startsWith(`, `.endsWith(`, `Object.assign`, `Array.prototype.find`, `Array.from`, `Number.isNaN` all return **0 in-scope files**.

The one real conformance gap is the cscript-ES3-parse rule: `.catch(` appears in **`yumi-brain.js:26`, `yumi-brain.js:123`** and **`yumi-ui.js:1249`**, and `.finally(` in **`yumi-ui.js:1254`** ‚Äî all genuine promise-chain calls. Per CLAUDE.md these two files are *intentionally* harness-exempt ("it cannot parse files using `.catch`/`.finally`‚Ä¶ Verify integrations.js, yumi-brain.js, and yumi-ui.js on the live deploy, not the harness"). They are not build-breaking, but the consequence (documented as a MEDIUM finding below) is that two of the largest, most logic-dense files (5,531 combined LOC, including the frozen Yumi gate) **cannot be statically parse-validated at all** before ship.

### 2. Parse status ‚Äî confirmed

Ran the committed cscript harnesses (each reads the live `js/` file via FileSystemObject + `new Function(src)`):

- `state.js` ‚Üí **PASS** (126,228 chars)
- `views.js` ‚Üí **PASS** (640,501 chars)
- `arc-constellation.js` ‚Üí **PASS** (86,671 chars)
- `tradition-forms-arc.js` ‚Üí **PASS** (23,659 chars)
- `integrations.js` ‚Üí **FAIL** "Expected identifier" (expected ‚Äî the documented exception)

I additionally parse-checked the un-harnessed files via temporary scratchpad harnesses: **`spotlight.js`, `writing-canvas.js`, `import-capture.js`, `voice-input.js`, `app.js` all PASS** ES3 parse, while `yumi-brain.js` and `yumi-ui.js` **FAIL** (the `.catch`/`.finally` above). Finding: five ES3-clean files (notably the 1,421-LOC `import-capture.js`) have **no committed parse-check harness**, so a regression there would only surface live.

### 3. Codebase shape & the views.js monolith

`wc -l js/*.js`:

| File | LOC | Note |
|---|---|---|
| views.js | 14,526 | **49.6% of all js; 53.4% of in-scope** |
| state.js | 2,944 | |
| yumi-brain.js | 2,800 | harness-exempt |
| integrations.js | 2,073 | (excluded) |
| yumi-ui.js | 1,928 | harness-exempt |
| arc-constellation.js | 1,849 | "invariant" file (Œî=0 across builds) |
| import-capture.js | 1,421 | IIFE module, no harness |
| writing-canvas.js | 659 | |
| spotlight.js | 457 | |
| tradition-forms-arc.js | 383 | |
| voice-input.js | 167 | |
| app.js | 56 | |
| arcs.js | 12 | dead stub |
| verify-engine.js | 11 | dead tombstone |

`views.js` is over half the client (192 top-level functions) ‚Äî a single point of merge contention the build protocol already flags ("views.js write-lane contends‚Ä¶").

### 4. Dead weight ‚Äî confirmed (~486 LOC of orphaned functions + two dead files)

**Dead files:**
- **`js/verify-engine.js`** ‚Äî NOT in `index.html` and NOT in `sw.js`'s precache list; referenced nowhere. Its own header calls it a "tombstone so that older clients holding a cached reference do not 404 during the praxis-v1 -> praxis-v2 cache rollover." Last touched `e58ab85` (2026-05-05); we are now at v3.150, so the rollover rationale is many versions stale. Safe to delete by its own terms.
- **`js/arcs.js`** ‚Äî IS loaded (`index.html:48`) and precached (`sw.js:25`), but is a 12-line empty IIFE whose only runtime effect is `console.log('arcs.js loaded')`. A stub since `ba03c4d` (2026-05-01, Stage 1.1) that was never implemented; it ships in the bundle and costs a request + a cache entry on every client.

**Orphaned top-level functions (defined once, called nowhere ‚Äî verified by full-corpus grep over `js/` + `index.html`, and confirmed absent from every export object):**

- `openScanReviewEditor` (`views.js:4406`, ~131 LOC) ‚Äî the old 6.2a inline scan-review editor; the live "Scan shelf" button (`views.js:2691`) routes through `handleShelfScanFile` ‚Üí `openBookReview`, which superseded it. Its `shelf-scan-review*` classes are referenced only inside this function (13 dead CSS rules in `assets/components.css`).
- `_stTreatment` (`arc-constellation.js:649`, 131 LOC), `_stRenderMarks` (`:1021`, 39 LOC), `_stSilhouette` (`:614`, 35 LOC) ‚Äî legacy constellation mark generators. The live renderer is `_stRenderShapes` (`:898`, called at `:1294` and `:1830`); these three are unreferenced leftovers from the verbatim mockup splice kept to preserve the file's Œî=0 invariant.
- `openManualLookup` (`views.js:5010`, 79 LOC) ‚Äî the "Add manually" verified-add flow; orphaned. Its `manual-lookup*` classes carry 13 dead CSS rules.
- `renderArtifactCard` (`views.js:10863`, 62 LOC) ‚Äî Stage 3.7 inline notebook artifact-card renderer; the `#artifact/<id>` route is served by the exported `renderArtifact` (`:8538`) instead. `notebook-artifact-card` carries 5 dead CSS rules and the `notebook-artifact-*` element family appears only here.
- `isBookDeletePending` (`state.js:866`, 9 LOC) ‚Äî a getter sibling to the used `markBookDeletePending`/`clearPendingBookDelete`; the "is pending?" query was authored but never consumed (partial API).

Each dead function with markup also strands its CSS (‚â•31 dead rules in `assets/components.css`), so the JS orphans understate the cleanup surface.

**Intentional dormant (NOT a defect, flagged for completeness):** `mountCommandConfirm` (`yumi-ui.js:500`) is unreferenced but explicitly documented as the dormant confirm-before-change scaffold for the deferred add-book-to-arc fast-follow ("the v1 command lane never writes‚Ä¶ this is never shown live").

### 5. Duplication

Logic duplication is minimal. The notable case is HTML/XML escaping, which exists in **three** near-identical forms: `_arcEscapeXml` (`arc-constellation.js:39`), `_portraitEsc` (`views.js:12461`), and a third inline `.replace(/&/g,‚Ä¶)` chain in `views.js` ‚Äî all doing the same five-entity escape. A shared `esc()` would consolidate them (the only meaningful divergence is `&apos;` vs `&#39;`). Conversely, markdown rendering is properly centralized: `wcRenderMarkdown` (`writing-canvas.js:36`) is the single renderer, consumed by `views.js:10707` ‚Äî no parallel implementation.

### 6. Substrate inconsistency

`'use strict'` placement is inconsistent: present in `app.js`, `arcs.js`, `spotlight.js`, `voice-input.js`, `yumi-brain.js`, `yumi-ui.js`, but **absent from the largest and most-active files** ‚Äî `views.js`, `state.js`, `arc-constellation.js`, `import-capture.js`, `writing-canvas.js`, `tradition-forms-arc.js`. The files most likely to leak an accidental global (14k-LOC views.js, 2.9k-LOC state.js) are the ones running without strict mode.

> Note: the documented "File load order" in CLAUDE.md (`state ‚Üí integrations ‚Üí yumi-brain ‚Üí arcs ‚Üí arc-constellation ‚Üí tradition-forms-arc ‚Üí voice-input ‚Üí yumi-ui ‚Üí views ‚Üí app`) does not match the actual `index.html` order (`state ‚Üí tradition-forms-arc ‚Üí arc-constellation ‚Üí integrations ‚Üí yumi-brain ‚Üí arcs ‚Üí voice-input ‚Üí yumi-ui ‚Üí spotlight ‚Üí writing-canvas ‚Üí views ‚Üí import-capture ‚Üí app`). This is documentation drift, not a runtime defect, and is out of scope for code findings ‚Äî recorded here as a cross-check observation.
