## PASS 3 ‚Äî Accessibility & design-system substrate

## Theme tokens, dual-ground mechanism, and token discipline

### Scope & method
Full read of `assets/theme.css` (484 lines) and a token-discipline sweep of `assets/components.css` (10,634 lines: `wc -l assets/theme.css assets/components.css`). All WCAG 2.1 ratios below were computed with the exact relative-luminance formula (sRGB linearization `((c+0.055)/1.055)^2.4` for `c>0.03928`, else `c/12.92`; `L=0.2126R+0.7152G+0.0722B`; contrast `(L1+0.05)/(L2+0.05)`) via an awk script over the resolved token hexes per ground. Normal-text AA = 4.5:1; large-text / UI = 3:1.

### 1. Token set (theme.css)
The palette is the June-2026 "Umber" re-skin and is well organized into named groups (theme.css:7-326):
- **Fonts (3):** `--font-serif`, `--font-body`, `--font-mono` (theme.css:9-11).
- **Dark study surfaces:** `--ground #2f1c0e`, `--ground-grad` (radial), `--surface-d #3e2814`, `--surface-d2 #4a3119`, `--sunk-d #241406`, `--dark-2 #2a1a0c` (theme.css:24-29).
- **Bright page surfaces:** `--page #f8f1e1`, `--page-2 #fcf6e8`, `--meta #9a7e4e`, `--text-d #f0e3c8`, `--muted #c2a87f` (theme.css:31-35).
- **Accents:** `--teal #2e8a93`, `--thread #c2a463`, `--gold-soft #e7c46a`, `--gold-ink #855410`, register colors `--register-marginalia(=teal)`, `--register-journal #7d6db0`, `--register-question #3a5a8a`, `--grad linear-gradient(92deg,#d2a23e,#2e8a93)` (theme.css:37-44, 298).
- **Inks (bright base):** `--ink #241710`, `--ink-2 #4d3b2a`, `--ink-3/--ink-4 ‚Üí var(--meta)`, `--br-deep #1c1209` (theme.css:60-68).
- **Re-pointed shared tokens:** `--gold/--gold-light/--gold-text ‚Üí var(--gold-ink)`, `--bg/--surface/--color-surface ‚Üí page tokens`, `--river #3a5a8a`, `--text-on-dark #fdfaf3` (theme.css:64-74).
- **Radii:** `--radius-sm 6px` (84), `--radius-md 10px` (272), `--radius-lg 16px` (85), `--radius-xl 22px` (299), `--radius-pill 999px` (309). **Spacing:** `--sp-1..6` (77-82).
- **Material system:** warm-brown two-layer shadow tiers `--shadow-1/-2/-yumi/-spotlight/-cover`, `--highlight-edge`, `--ease`, `--motion-base 350ms`, `--field-presence 0.22` (theme.css:248-287). The A3.1 rule is documented in-file: "NEVER rgba(0,0,0,...) per A3.1" (theme.css:246).
- **Frozen renderer palettes:** 16 `--subtheory-N` + `-edge` identity fills with a `[data-st-palette="muted"]`/`"colorful"` global remap (theme.css:186-225, 444-484); 9 `--tradition-*-halo` constellation feeds (theme.css:168-184). These are intentionally out of dual-ground scope (theme.css:18-21).

### 2. Dual-ground mechanism (verified)
`:root` carries the **bright-page** values; a single override block re-points the ground-sensitive tokens to the dark study set (theme.css:336-361). It is keyed off `[data-ground="dark"]` plus the always-dark floating chrome selectors `.app-nav, .yumi-bloom, .yumi-panel, .spotlight-panel`. The block remaps **18 declarations** (`sed -n '336,361p' | grep -cE '^\s+--[a-z]'` ‚Üí 18): `--ink, --ink-2, --ink-3, --ink-4, --surface, --surface-2, --color-surface, --bg, --bg-2, --border, --line-2, --wash, --glass, --glass-2, --sunk, --gold, --gold-light, --gold-text`. The attribute is set per route in `js/views.js:369-371` (`umberGroundDark = { home, books, arcs, arc, account }` ‚Üí `dark`, everything else `bright`). The page-ground pseudo swaps with it (`body[data-ground="dark"]::before` ‚Üí `--ground-grad`, theme.css:435-437).

**The gold split is correct by design:** `--gold-text` stays muted `--gold-ink #855410` on the light page (**5.95:1 PASS**) and brightens to `--gold-soft #e7c46a` on dark (**8.23:1 PASS**) ‚Äî theme.css:356-360 documents that the bright `#d2a23e` "fails AA (2.08) and gold-ink passes (5.7)" on the light page. This is the model the failing tokens below should have followed but did not.

### 3. Contrast failures (per ground)
The dual-ground remap covers the ink/surface/gold families but **omits `--river`, `--question-color`, `--marginalia-color`/teal, `--journal-color`, `--wordmark`, `--gold-soft`, and `--danger`** ‚Äî so these resolve to one value on both grounds, and several fall below AA on the ground where they are actually painted.

| Foreground | Background | Ground | Ratio | Verdict |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `--wordmark`/`--gold-soft #e7c46a` | `--page #f8f1e1` / `--surface #fcf6e8` | bright | **1.49‚Äì1.56:1** | FAIL (both) |
| `--river`/`--question-color #3a5a8a` | `--surface-d #3e2814` | dark | **1.98:1** | FAIL (both) |
| `--register-journal #7d6db0` | `--surface-d #3e2814` | dark | **3.09:1** | FAIL normal |
| `--marginalia-color`/teal `#2e8a93` | `--surface-d #3e2814` | dark | **3.41:1** | FAIL normal |
| `--meta`(=`--ink-3`/`--ink-4`) `#9a7e4e` | `--page`/`--surface` | bright | **3.41‚Äì3.56:1** | FAIL normal |
| `--danger #c2603a` | `--page` / `--ground` | both | **3.71 / 3.89:1** | FAIL normal |
| `--marginalia-color`/teal `#2e8a93` | `--surface #fcf6e8` | bright | **3.77:1** | FAIL normal |
| `--on-teal #06241a` | `--teal #2e8a93` fill | n/a | **4.06:1** | borderline (OK large/UI) |
| `--br-deep #1c1209` | `--grad` end-stop `#2e8a93` | n/a | **4.54:1** | PASS (endpoint only) |

Each failure is a real text use, not a theoretical pairing:
- **`--wordmark` on bright (1.49:1)** ‚Äî `.notebook-entry-add-to-arc` (components.css:4207), and two more at 4288 and 4781, render this as a 12px text link on the bright notebook page: near-invisible pale-gold on cream.
- **`--meta` on bright (3.56:1)** ‚Äî `.book-detail-meta` is 11px `--ink-3` (components.css:2685-2691) on the bright book-detail page; `.notebook-entry-ts` is 10px `--ink-4` (components.css:4132-4135). `--ink-3`/`--ink-4` are used as `color:` 223 and 66 times respectively (`grep -cE 'color:\s*var\(--ink-3\)'`).
- **teal on bright (3.77:1)** ‚Äî `.about .yumi-col--is h3` (components.css:9568) at 10.5px uppercase mono.
- **`--river` on dark (1.98:1)** and **teal on dark (3.41:1)** ‚Äî `.ground-chip.web`/`.ground-chip.theme` chips inside the dark Yumi panel (components.css:425-433) use these as 10px label text; `--river`/`--question-color`/`--marginalia-color`/`--journal-color` are never in the dark override block.

`--gold-text`/`--gold` text on bright passes (5.95:1) because those ARE remapped ‚Äî the fix pattern already exists in-file.

### 4. Token discipline in components.css (mostly excellent, a few drifts)
Token usage is strong: **2,900 `var(--‚Ä¶)` references** vs **0 live hardcoded hex** (`grep -oE '#[0-9a-fA-F]{3,8}' assets/components.css | wc -l` ‚Üí 2, both inside a comment at line 7589; named colors `white`/`black` ‚Üí 0). Remaining literals:
- **23 raw `rgb()/rgba()` literals** (`grep -oE 'rgba?\([0-9]' | wc -l`). Most are the established warm-brown shadow brown `rgba(58,40,16,‚Ä¶)` (same literal the `--shadow-spotlight` token uses, theme.css:254) and inset highlights `rgba(255,250,230,.5)` ‚Äî defensible. But several duplicate tokens or violate A3.1:
  - **A3.1 pure-black shadows** at components.css:1696 (`rgba(0,0,0,0.08)`), 9786, 9787 (`.btn-primary` `rgba(0,0,0,.28/.34)`) ‚Äî the design canon forbids `rgba(0,0,0,‚Ä¶)`; warm `--shadow-*` tokens exist.
  - **`--scrim` duplicated verbatim:** components.css:9989 `background:rgba(15,9,4,.6)` is byte-identical to `--scrim: rgba(15,9,4,.6)` (theme.css:57); components.css:10074 uses the same base at `.5`.
  - **Stale-hue register literals:** `.notebook-entry-tag-m` border `rgba(29,143,104,.45)` (components.css:4123) = `#1d8f68`, the **pre-Umber teal**, while the tag's own text uses `var(--marginalia-color)` = `#2e8a93` (new teal) ‚Äî the border and text are now different hues. Likewise `.notebook-entry-tag-q` border `rgba(39,86,106,.45)` (components.css:4129) = `#27566a`, the **old `--river`**, while `--river`/`--question-color` is now `#3a5a8a`. The Yumi-panel hairline `rgba(29,143,104,.35)` (components.css:3236) is the same stale teal.
- **18 raw-px radii that duplicate existing tokens:** 16√ó `border-radius:10px` (= `--radius-md`, e.g. components.css:877, 1176, 2765, 6712, 6984) and 2√ó `border-radius:6px` (= `--radius-sm`, components.css:3810, 10567), against 206 token-based radii (`grep -cE 'border-radius:\s*var\('`).

These are low-stakes drift on an otherwise disciplined stylesheet; the contrast gaps in ¬ß3 are the substantive findings.

## Accessibility & Responsive Substrate (`assets/components.css` 10,634 lines ¬∑ `js/views.js` 14,526 lines)

This area audits the inspectable a11y/responsive substrate: tap-target sizing, focus visibility, keyboard operability, ARIA, reduced-motion, breakpoints, and type/motion consistency. The substrate is **partially conscientious** ‚Äî there is a genuine `:focus-visible` allow-list, a per-component reduced-motion strategy, three properly-marked modal dialogs, and an exemplary keyboard pattern (`role=button`+`tabindex=0`+`keydown`) on shelf filter rows ‚Äî but coverage is **uneven**: newer surfaces (segmented controls, notebook tabs, Yumi panel chrome, import-capture overlay, reader-portrait toggles) were shipped without inheriting these patterns, and a global `--meta`-resolved ink token fails AA contrast on the light ground.

### 1. Tap targets (WCAG 2.5.5 / 2.5.8 ‚Äî target ~44√ó44 CSS px)

Multiple **interactive** controls render well below a 44px touch target, with no `min-height`/`min-width` compensation:

| Control | Rule | Size |
|---|---|---|
| `.app-nav-hamburger` (PRIMARY mobile nav) | components.css:3871 `font-size:28px; padding:0; line-height:1`, shown `display:block` at ‚â§759 (5416) | **~28√ó28px** |
| `.seg-opt` (segmented control, ~7 surfaces) | components.css:9685/9839/9942/10039/10106 `padding:6px 12-14px; font-size:11px`, no `min-height` | **~23px tall** |
| `.notebook .nb-tab` (notebook section nav) | components.css:9839 `padding:6px 12px; font-size:11px` | **~23px tall** |
| `.rm-iconbtn` (reader-model edit/delete `<button>`) | components.css:9740 `width:26px;height:26px` | **26√ó26px** |
| `.ic-close` (import overlay close `<button>`) | components.css:10280 `width:32px;height:32px` | **32√ó32px** |
| `.yumi-panel .yumi-icon-btn` (send/mic) | components.css:10152 `width:36px;height:36px` | **36√ó36px** |
| `.app-nav-link` | components.css:681 `padding:8px 12px; font-size:13.5px` | **~32px tall** |
| `.app-nav-profile` (avatar chip) | components.css:719 `width:34px;height:34px` | **34√ó34px** |
| Desktop nav links (‚â•760) | components.css:779 `padding:6px 2px; font-size:12px` | **~24px tall; ~2px horiz pad** |

The Yumi FAB orb (`.yumi-bloom-orb`, components.css:34 `56√ó56`) is the lone large primary target. The hamburger is the most serious: it is the *only* nav affordance on mobile and is a bare 28px glyph.

### 2. Focus visibility

`outline:none`/`outline:0` appears **27 times** (`grep -ciE 'outline:\s*(none|0)'` = 27; control `app-nav-link:focus-visible` matched = 1). This is **not** blanket focus suppression ‚Äî there is no global `*`/`button` reset, and the removals fall into two acceptable patterns plus one gap:

- **Correctly replaced**: a 27-selector `:focus-visible` allow-list (components.css:3941-3970) restores `outline: 2px solid var(--river)` for shelf/book-detail/notebook-settings controls, and `.yumi-bloom:focus{outline:none}` is paired with `:focus-visible` (components.css:61-66). 85 `:focus-visible` rules exist total.
- **Intentional typing focus**: most `outline:none` sit on `<input>`/`<textarea>`/contenteditable (e.g. components.css:9266, 9344, 9873, 10026, 10047) where a border treatment carries focus.
- **Gap**: newer interactive classes have **no `:focus-visible` rule at all** ‚Äî `.seg-opt`, `.nb-tab`, `.yumi-icon-btn`, `.ic-close`, `.rm-iconbtn`, `.st-mark-chip`, `.arc-card` (all returned empty from `grep '\.<sel>:focus'`). These fall back to the UA default ring, which is inconsistent with the house `--river` ring but is not invisible ‚Äî except where the element is a styled `<div>`/`<span>` that the UA does not ring.

### 3. Keyboard operability

189 `addEventListener('click'` vs **27** `keydown/keypress/keyup` handlers in views.js (`grep -cE`). Core navigation is safe ‚Äî book cards (views.js:3610,3708) and arc cards (views.js:2324) are real `<a href>`, the create tiles are `<button>` ‚Äî so most click handlers ride native semantics. The app even has an **exemplary** accessible-row pattern: shelf filter rows get `role=button`+`tabindex=0`+`onShelfFilterRowClick`+`onShelfFilterRowKeydown` (views.js:2986-2996), and notebook privacy toggles bind both click and an Enter/Space keydown (views.js:11011-11020).

The defect is **incomplete adoption** on the reader-portrait surface:
- The portrait master toggle is rendered `<div data-act="rmtoggle" tabindex="0" role="button">` (views.js:13836) ‚Äî i.e. it *advertises* itself to AT as a focusable button ‚Äî but its handler at views.js:13857 is **click-only**; there is no keydown bridge. A keyboard user can focus it and press Enter/Space to no effect.
- The portrait offer chips `<span data-act="confirm|rename|reject">` (views.js:13590) and `data-act="suggest"` (views.js:13611,13617) are click-only spans with no `tabindex` ‚Äî unreachable and unactivatable by keyboard. Their delegated handler is click-only (views.js:13731).

### 4. ARIA

views.js ARIA inventory (`grep -oE 'aria-[a-z]+' | sort | uniq -c`): `aria-label` √ó34, `aria-hidden` √ó13, `aria-pressed` √ó11, `aria-checked` √ó4, `aria-selected` √ó3, `aria-modal` √ó3, `aria-labelledby` √ó3, `aria-expanded` √ó1; `role=` √ó11 (button √ó2, group √ó2, img √ó4, tablist √ó1). `index.html` is well-formed: `lang="en"` (line 2), viewport with `viewport-fit=cover` (5), nav search `aria-label` (21), hamburger `aria-label` (35), decorative spans `aria-hidden` (22,31,32).

Three views.js modals are correctly marked `role=dialog`+`aria-modal=true` (st-picker 6823-6825 with `aria-label` + focus-on-open at 6966; 7045-7046; 7122-7123). **Gaps:**
- **Import-capture overlay** (`#ic-overlay`, a fixed full-screen modal, import-capture.js:402): **no `role=dialog`, no `aria-modal`, no Escape-key handler, no focus management** ‚Äî it closes only on scrim-click (407) or close button. It is the single largest un-ARIA'd modal surface.
- **Yumi chat panel** has `role=dialog` (yumi-ui.js:1009) but **no `aria-modal`** (only the takeover overlay at 1829-1830 carries both).
- **No focus trap** on any views.js dialog or the Yumi chat panel; the *only* focus trap in the codebase is the lens panel (yumi-ui.js:1887-1888). Modals therefore leak Tab focus to the page behind them.

### 5. prefers-reduced-motion

Motion **is** gated ‚Äî `prefers-reduced-motion` appears **21 times** (`grep -ic` = 21), against ~73 `transition:` and 49 `animation:` declarations / 31 `@keyframes`. Gating is **per-component** (Bloom states 101-109/178-191/505-506, arc drift 6057-6067, account-panel 7970, portrait-breathe 8199-8200, lens 9164-9166, scanline 9297-9298, about-spin 9631-9633, import-capture 10349-10351, writing-canvas 10572/10602). There is **no global `* { animation-duration: 0.01ms }` reset**, so any animation not explicitly named is **not** reduced ‚Äî most visibly the route-transition `#app > * { animation: route-fade-in ‚Ä¶ both }` (components.css:5789-5791) and `fade-and-rise` (5801), which fire on **every render** and are ungated.

### 6. Responsiveness ‚Äî breakpoint inventory

The CSS is desktop-first (base rules = desktop) with the mobile fold at 760, per CLAUDE.md. True media-query breakpoints (`grep -E '@media.*[0-9]+px'` ‚Äî the dozens of small `max-width: NNNpx` hits are CSS *properties*, not queries):

- `min-width: 760px` √ó4 (the desktop step-ups: nav pill 761, book-detail 2077, 4571, etc.)
- `max-width: 759px` √ó12 (the mobile block)
- `max-width: 720px` √ó2 (legacy ‚Äî arcs-create / arc-card / subtheory, per canon "leave alone")
- `max-width: 1099px` √ó1 (shelf-grid step)
- `max-width: 639px` √ó1, `max-width: 499px` √ó1

Coverage is reasonable, but the **portrait/galaxy reader-portrait surface and the import-capture overlay have no `759` mobile block** in components.css (grep of `9380-10231` mobile blocks shows notebook/shelf/st-page/arcfield/about but not portrait galaxy internals or `.ic-panel` reflow) ‚Äî these will rely on intrinsic sizing and are likely to break narrow. [requires live verification at 390px]

### 7. Type / motion consistency

**Type substrate is clean.** All 569 `font-family` declarations in components.css resolve to `var(--font-serif|body|mono)` ‚Äî the single non-token hit (components.css:6072) is a comment. Tokens are correctly defined in theme.css:9-11 (Cormorant Garamond / DM Sans / DM Mono with proper fallbacks) and the fonts are preconnected + loaded in index.html:10-12. No raw font-name drift, no rogue system-serif misuse.

### Contrast (AA, computed)

`--ink-3` and `--ink-4` both resolve to `--meta` = `#9a7e4e` (theme.css:33,62,63). On the light page surface `--surface`/`--surface-2` = `#fcf6e8`, that is **3.56:1** (computed) ‚Äî **fails WCAG AA (4.5:1) for normal text**, passing only the 3:1 large-text bar. `--ink-3` is used **223 times** and `--ink-4` **83 times** (`grep -c`), heavily on *small* mono meta/eyebrow/label text: `.book-review-eyebrow` 10.5px (9305), `.about .yumi-eyebrow` 10.5px (9556), `.about .seg-opt` 11.5px (9685). Primary inks pass (`--ink` 16.17:1, `--ink-2` 9.87:1) and the dark-study palette passes (`--muted` on `--surface-d` 6.06:1, `--text-d` on `--ground` 12.78:1), so the failure is specifically meta/label text on the bright ground.


---

## PASS 4 ‚Äî Per-surface deep notes

## Home Surface (`#home`, dark ground)

**Entry:** `renderHome()` at `js/views.js:606` (117 LOC, single definition); routed from `renderRoute()` `js/views.js:569`. Reached from the wordmark and a top-nav "Home" link (`index.html:19,25`) and is the cold-open default (`js/app.js:14-16`). Dark ground is set via `umberGroundDark` map at `js/views.js:369-371` (`home:1`), so the `[data-ground="dark"]` token remap (`theme.css:336-361`) resolves on this surface. Active-link mapping handles `home` (`js/views.js:391-393`).

### IS ‚Äî verified current state

**Structure.** Two stacked blocks inside `.home-page > .home-hero` + `.home-preview`. Hero = mono eyebrow ("A reading practice"), serif H1 ("Your reading becomes " + gradient-clip `.accent` "theory."), italic serif sub, and a `.home-cta` row of two anchors. Preview = a cap row (`.dot` + eyebrow "A living constellation") plus either a live inert mini-constellation embed OR a static fallback line.

**CTA wiring is sound.** `ctaPrimary` ‚Üí `#books` (`renderShelf()`, `js/views.js:516-525`); `ctaSecondary` ‚Üí `#arcs` (`renderArcsPage()`, `js/views.js:527-538`). Both are plain `<a href>` anchors navigating via the hash router ‚Äî no JS handlers, no dead buttons. They correctly adopt the canonical `.btn`/`.btn-primary`/`.btn-ghost` primitives (`components.css:9778-9789`), which are dual-ground-tokenized.

**Dark-ground contrast PASSES across the board** (WCAG 2.1, computed): hero eyebrow + sub `--ink-3`=`--muted #c2a87f` on `--ground #2f1c0e` = **7.11** (passes AA 4.5 even for the 10.5px eyebrow); title `--text-d #f0e3c8`/ground = **12.78**; gradient accent `--grad` endpoints teal `#2e8a93` = **4.00** / gold `#d2a23e` = **6.94** on ground (both clear the 3.0 large-text bar for the clamp(40‚Äì82px) display title); fallback `.home-preview-line` = **9.47**; preview eyebrow on the panel fill = **6.06**. No contrast finding on Home.

**Token discipline is near-clean.** 32 `var()` uses in the home CSS blocks (`components.css:814-976`); exactly **one** raw color literal ‚Äî the `.home-preview` box-shadow `rgba(58,40,16,.55)` (`components.css:914`), consistent with the codebase's established raw-rgba shadow pattern.

**Mobile stack (canon J) is satisfied ‚Äî via the live class, not the named helper.** `@media (max-width:759px)` sets `.home-cta { flex-direction:column }` (`components.css:5717-5719`); `.home-cta` is a live class, so the buttons stack. Column flex default `align-items:stretch` plus `.btn`'s own `justify-content:center` yields full-width, centered-label buttons. Hero font scales via `.home-title { clamp(40px,8vw,82px) }` (`components.css:968`).

### REGRESSIONS / DIVERGENCE ‚Äî verified

**1. The Batch 4A home CSS is dead and superseded ‚Äî a stale parallel substrate.** `renderHome` emits `.home-title`, `.accent`, `.home-sub`, `.eyebrow home-eyebrow`, `.btn .btn-primary`, `.btn .btn-ghost`. But `components.css:837-903` still defines `.home-hero-title`, `.home-hero-accent`, `.home-hero-sub`, `.home-cta-primary`, `.home-cta-secondary` ‚Äî **0 JS references each** (`grep -rl ... js/` = 0; control: `home-title`/`home-cta` = 1). These were the original 4A markup classes, replaced by the Umber port (`components.css:961-976`) + `.btn` adoption, but the old rules were never removed. ~10 dead rule lines. This is the same dead-substrate / IS-vs-intent drift the CLAUDE.md design canon warns about.

**2. The mobile font-size override targets a dead class.** `@media (max-width:759px) .home-hero-title { font-size:52px }` (`components.css:5724-5727`) and `.home-cta-primary/.home-cta-secondary { justify-content:center }` (`5720-5722`) all reference dead classes ‚Äî the intended 52px mobile cap and explicit label-centering never apply. No user-visible breakage (clamp gives ~40px; `.btn` already centers), but the canon-J mobile intent is implemented against ghosts.

**3. The "presentational only ‚Äî no data read" header comment is stale.** `js/views.js:601-602` ("no marks, no constellation canvas, no data read"). The later FINALE embed (added below) reads `state.seeds`, `state.arcs`, and `state.subTheories` via `_arcDetailBuildSubTheoryData` (`js/views.js:681-710`). The comment predates the embed and now misdescribes the function.

**4. The "live mini-constellation" embed is effectively unreachable on shipped data.** The embed branch (`js/views.js:689-710`) only renders when the seed arc has ‚â•1 sub-theory. The seed arc is migrate-created with `bookIds` (5 seed books) but **zero sub-theories** (`js/state.js:2593-2613`); no code seeds a sub-theory against `seedArcId`. So `_arcDetailBuildSubTheoryData(seedArc).subTheories.length` is 0 for every fresh user, and the static fallback line (`js/views.js:712-716`) is what ships. The embed only activates if a user manually attaches a sub-theory to the seeded "Pedagogy of Desire" arc ‚Äî an unlikely path. The headline "A living constellation" preview is therefore aspirational, not the default experience. (Requires live verification to confirm rendered output on a populated account.)

### Notes
- `.home-page` (1080) > `.home-hero` (880) max-widths nest correctly; both 4A and Umber `.home-hero`/`.home-cta` base rules apply per-property with Umber winning overlaps ‚Äî no broken cascade.
- The seed arc is sentinel-owned (`userId:'__praxis_seed__'`), so the embed reading all its sub-theories without an `isPrivate` filter is by design (no private-leak path here).

## Shelf / Categories (route `#books` ‚Üí `renderShelf()`, dark ground)

### Summary
The Shelf is the most heavily-iterated surface in the app (renderShelf alone spans `js/views.js:2522`‚Äì`3603`, ~1080 lines, plus ~1700 lines of sub-renderers). It is functionally rich and largely sound: a deduped index-driven render, a six-section single-select filter rail (status / lenses(genre) / manual-themes / categories / author / search), Covers|List dual views, a self-healing cover walk, two camera paths (native `BarcodeDetector` + lazy `@zxing` fallback) with an always-present ISBN type-in, photo shelf-scan ‚Üí vision-proxy ‚Üí resolver ‚Üí review, bulk add, and a one-time "Tidy library" de-dupe/cover pass. **The single most important IS finding contradicts both the task brief and the project memory: the shelf-categories Stage 2 (real LLM classification) is fully built, wired, and persisted ‚Äî it is NOT a "classifying‚Ä¶" placeholder.** The residual issues are debt and design-substrate drift, not broken core behavior.

### IS ‚Äî verified current state

**Categories grouping is fully implemented (not a stub).** The sidebar carries a `[Lenses | Categories]` segmented toggle (`getShelfGrouping`/`setShelfGrouping`, key `praxis_shelf_grouping`, default `lenses`, allow-list coerced ‚Äî `js/views.js:300`‚Äì`313`, built `3096`‚Äì`3125`). Picking **Categories** runs a lazy, cached, batched classifier: `classifyBookLocal` (`js/state.js:600`) resolves cached-label ‚Üí `rawCategories` BISAC keyword map (`RAW_CATEGORY_MAP`, 50+ ordered entries `js/state.js:528`+) ‚Üí `null`; any `null` book is sent ONCE to `classifyBooksViaLLM` (`js/integrations.js:1846`, model `claude-sonnet-4-6`, batches of 20, temp 0, fail-soft to `Uncategorized` on any transport/parse miss), the result cached on `book.category`, persisted in ONE batched `markBooksDirty()`+`saveState()` (`js/views.js:3177`‚Äì`3194`). The 17-category taxonomy + `Uncategorized` is the single source of truth (`SHELF_CATEGORIES` `js/state.js:484`, validated by `isValidCategoryLabel` `:517`, re-used to build `CLASSIFY_SYSTEM` `js/integrations.js:1759`). `category` is in the `ensureBookFields` chokepoint (`js/state.js:411`) and `ensureBookFieldsAll`, so it survives the REPLACE-on-auth Firestore merge cross-device.

**The classifier hang is guarded.** Because `classifyBooksViaLLM` has no timeout/AbortController, a watchdog (`js/views.js:3169`, deadline `20000 + ceil(n/20)*20000`ms) bumps a generation token (`shelfClassifyGen`), clears `shelfCategorizing`, and re-renders so a hung pass self-recovers ‚Äî a genuine improvement over the unguarded proxy calls elsewhere in the app.

**Render is dedupe-safe (v3.112 lesson honored).** `renderShelf` clears `host.innerHTML=''` first (`js/views.js:2525`); the head count (`2570`‚Äì`2590`), the lens/category/status counts (`lcArr`, `2864`‚Äì`2912`), and the grid (`3408`‚Äì`3419`) all read the SAME source ‚Äî the signed-in user's `state.userBooks[uid].bookIds` index, falling back to raw `state.books` only when signed out. **Rendered count therefore equals the indexed (deduped) count by construction**; orphan/duplicate `state.books` records cannot inflate counts or double-paint rows.

**Filter pass is strict and AND-composed** (`js/views.js:3433`‚Äì`3491`): `author`/`genre`/`status`/`tradition`/`category` exact-equality + a case-insensitive substring `search`. `categoryOk` calls `classifyBookLocal(fb)` (O(1) on cache hit). Single-select with exclusive cross-section clear (`toggleShelfFilter` `3949`). Rows are `role=button`, `tabindex=0`, with paired click+`Enter`/`Space` keydown handlers (`onShelfFilterRowClick`/`onShelfFilterRowKeydown` `3971`/`4016`) ‚Äî keyboard-reachable. Empty-state copy switches on `filterActive` (which correctly includes `category` `3517`).

**Cover self-heal + barcode are robust.** `buildSelfHealingCover` (`js/views.js:5098`) walks `coverCandidates`, marks `coverBrokenIds` on exhaustion, swaps in a typographic "cover pending" placeholder (real `<span>` for a11y), and clears the broken-mark on a later successful load. `openBarcodeScanner` (`4824`) degrades cleanly: native detector ‚Üí lazy `@zxing` (`loadZxingLibrary` `4798`, idempotent, queued, CDN, never precached) ‚Üí ever-present ISBN type-in; every camera failure path writes a user-visible status and never blocks. Scan-shelf (`handleShelfScanFile` `5852`) has complete error coverage (downscale error, non-200, parse error, network error, empty-titles ‚Äî each restores the button and shows status).

**Persistence is P0-safe on add.** Single-add (`openShelfEditor` `4187`) and bulk-add (`processBulkLines` `4537`) both `ensureBookFields` + `markBookPending(uid,id)` + `markBooksDirty`+`saveState` per write, then background cover/metadata backfill that only patches blank fields and re-renders only when still on `#books`.

### REGRESSIONS / DEAD WEIGHT / DRIFT

- **Stale memory + brief.** The project memory note "[Shelf categories Stage 1B] ‚Ä¶ Categories = 'classifying‚Ä¶' placeholder. Stage 2 (real classify) NEXT" and the task brief's "the 'classifying...' placeholder (categories Stage 2 not built)" are both **out of date** ‚Äî Stage 2 is shipped (evidence above). This is a documentation regression, not code.
- **~18 stranded legacy CSS rules** for `.shelf-scan-btn` / `.shelf-new-book-bulk` / `.shelf-resolve-covers-btn` (`assets/components.css:1166`‚Äì`1244`, `5611`‚Äì`5656`, focus/active blocks `3944`‚Äì`4003`). The toolbar buttons now carry BOTH the legacy class AND `.chip` (e.g. `className='chip shelf-scan-btn'` `js/views.js:2690`); the `.chip` block (`components.css:9792`) wins for the properties it sets by source order, and the legacy `grid-column` declarations are inert under the flex `.shelf-toolbar`. The Umber-port header comment (`components.css:9928`) explicitly flags these as "go dead ‚Äî drift." Confirmed dead/overridden weight + a maintenance hazard (edits to the legacy block silently no-op).
- **Toolbar exceeds canon ¬ß4-E.** Canon prescribes ONE primary + Covers|List + **3 quiet chips** (Scan shelf / Bulk add / Resolve covers). The live toolbar renders **5 chips** (adds *Scan barcode* and *Tidy library* ‚Äî `js/views.js:2690`/`2710`/`2719`/`2730`/`2746`) plus the primary, the seg, a *Filters* button, and the search well. The declutter goal is only partially met; on a narrow viewport the flex-wrap toolbar becomes a dense multi-row cluster (no mobile-specific collapse for the chips ‚Äî see ledger).
- **Re-classify clears categories app-wide, not shelf-scoped.** The "Re-classify" handler iterates `for (rbid in state.books)` globally (`js/views.js:3268`), wiping `category` on every record in the shared map ‚Äî including books not in the signed-in user's `bookIds` index. Low blast radius (forces re-classification only) but it is a scope mismatch with the deduped read model the rest of renderShelf is careful to use.
- **No add-time dedupe.** Single-add has no existence check at all; bulk-add dedupes only within the current paste batch (`seenIsbns` `js/views.js:4543`). Re-adding the same ISBN/title across sessions mints a new `genBookId` record ‚Üí a genuine duplicate in `state.books`. Mitigated (not prevented) by "Tidy library"; this is the same family as the v3.112 duplication lesson, here user-initiated.
- **Doc/code drift in `classifyBookLocal` comment.** The state.js header says the resolver is "cached ‚Üí seed ‚Üí keyword ‚Üí null" (`js/state.js:479`, `594`) but the function has no seed step ‚Äî only cached ‚Üí `rawCategories` keyword ‚Üí null (`:600`‚Äì`616`). Cosmetic.
- **Dead `.shelf-seg-option` rules** (`assets/components.css:1350`,`1362`) ‚Äî a pre-Umber segmented-control class with no live producer (the live segs use `.seg`/`.seg-opt`).

### DIVERGENCE from spec
Per ¬ß4-E above (5 chips vs 3). The decluttered primary+seg+quiet structure otherwise matches; tokens are wired correctly (chips `var(--wash)`/`var(--ink-2)`/`var(--border)`; segs `var(--grad)` active fill; dark-ground remap via `[data-ground="dark"]` set for `#books` at `js/views.js:369`).

## Arcs Page / List (`#arcs`, dark ground)

**Route:** `#arcs` ‚Üí `renderRoute` (js/views.js:537) ‚Üí `renderArcsPage()` (js/views.js:2244). Body data-ground is set to `dark` for `arcs` (js/views.js:369-371), so all token resolution below uses the `[data-ground="dark"]` override block (theme.css:341-360).

### IS ‚Äî verified current behavior

**Page structure (js/views.js:2244-2488).** `renderArcsPage` clears `#app` and builds, in order: an `.arcs-head` block (eyebrow "Constellations" + `<h1 class="arcs-title">Arcs</h1>` + an italic `.arcs-teach` teaching paragraph, 2256-2277); the `#notebook-arc-editor-host` mount point for the shared `openArcEditor` (2282-2284); a signed-in-only "Your arcs" section (2292-2379); and an always-rendered "Arcs to learn from / examples" section (2404-2485). The header "+ Create an arc" button is intentionally dropped ‚Äî create is reached only via the dashed start-tile inside the Your-arcs grid (2356-2376), so **a signed-out visitor has no create affordance at all** (the entire `if (arcsUser)` block, including the start tile, is gated on a user ‚Äî 2293).

**Arc card = thumb + title + desc + computed mono meta (canon G ‚Äî IMPLEMENTED).** Both the live "Your arcs" cards (2324-2353) and the seeded "A Pedagogy of Desire" example card (2425-2453) build: `_arcCardThumb()` (a decorative inline-SVG spark banner, 2229-2242) ‚Üí `.arc-card-body` (title + optional description) ‚Üí `.arc-card-meta` populated by `_arcCardMetaText(_arcCardCounts(...))`. The 5-cover thumbnail row called out as dropped in canon G is genuinely gone ‚Äî the JS emits no `arc-card-covers`/`arc-card-cover` (grep below). `_arcCardCounts` (2185-2211) computes books = `arc.bookIds.length`, sub-theories = a full scan of `state.subTheories` filtered by `arcId`, marginalia = `arc.entryIds` whose resolved `entry.register === 'marginalia'`; `_arcCardMetaText` (2215-2224) always shows books + sub-theories and appends marginalia only when > 0. Counts are display-only aggregation; no data-model change. The entryIds shape (`{id, addedAt}`) is read correctly via `arcRec.entryIds[i].id` (2203).

**Examples section (js/views.js:2404-2485).** Two cards, no parent `<h2>` competing with the page `<h1>` (by design, 2381-2403): the live `Pedagogy of Desire` card reads `state.seeds.pedagogyOfDesire` with a triple guard (missing seeds map / missing entry / missing arc record all skip cleanly, 2419-2424), and a hardcoded illustrated `Pedagogy of Flow` `<div>` (no href, no click target ‚Äî 2456-2483) whose meaning is carried by an `.arc-card-label` "Illustrated example" tag + `opacity:0.78` (components.css:1707-1721).

**Arc-detail List view renders a proper list, NOT blown-up covers (the v3.112 regression is NOT present here).** The List branch of `renderArcDetail` (js/views.js:9915-10002) merges `arc.bookIds` + `arc.entryIds` into one `addedAt`-sorted stream and renders each as `renderShelfBook` (the standard shelf card) or `renderNotebookEntry`, with `renderArcMissingMember` placeholders for unresolvable ids (9964, 9995). No covers are scaled up; the sub-theory constellation lives only in the Web branch.

**Sub-theory absence in List view (IS, structural).** The arc-detail header sub-meta line counts "N sub-theories" (js/views.js:9562-9585) and the Arcs-page card meta line counts them too, but **sub-theories are never rendered as list rows in the List view** ‚Äî the List branch iterates only `bookIds`/`entryIds` (9924-9943), never `state.subTheories`. Sub-theories surface only in the Web/constellation view and on the dedicated `renderSubTheoryPage`. This is a count-without-a-list gap, not a regression.

**Contrast on the dark ground PASSES AA** (computed below): card meta `--gold`‚Üí`#d2a23e` on card `--surface`‚Üí`#3e2814` = 5.91; description `--ink-3`‚Üí`#c2a87f` = 6.06; title `--ink`‚Üí`#f0e3c8` = 10.88; teaching paragraph on ground `#2f1c0e` = 7.11.

### REGRESSIONS / DIVERGENCE

**Mobile 1-up collapse is dead ‚Äî canon F (1-up mobile / 3-up desktop) is violated.** The grid container class emitted by JS is `arcs-grid` (js/views.js:2319, 2416), with `arcs-yours` / `arcs-examples` assigned as **ids** (`.id =`, js/views.js:2320, 2417). The desktop-first base rule `.arcs-grid { grid-template-columns:repeat(3,1fr) }` (components.css:1821) is the only rule that targets the live container, and it has **no `max-width:759px` override**. The mobile collapse rule that exists ‚Äî `.arcs-yours, .arcs-examples { grid-template-columns:1fr }` inside the `@media (max-width:759px)` block (components.css:5730-5733) ‚Äî uses **class** selectors that match nothing (those names are ids on the DOM). Result: the Arcs page stays 3-up at phone widths. At 390px this leaves ‚âà98px per column (page padding 2√ó24 + 2√ó24 gap = 96px of 342px), with a fixed 140px-tall thumb and 16-18px body padding ‚Äî text wraps/overflows, and because the columns are `1fr` (not `minmax(0,1fr)`) grid items cannot shrink below content min-width, risking horizontal page overflow. The comment at components.css:1584-1585 ("1-up on mobile (the max-width:759 override)") and the canon-F comment at 5729 both describe behavior the selectors do not deliver. The legacy pre-Umber class-selector grids `.arcs-examples`/`.arcs-yours` (components.css:1586-1601) are likewise dead (JS uses ids).

**Illustrated-card label is mis-inset.** `.arc-card-label` (components.css:1712-1721) has `margin:0 0 12px 0` (no horizontal inset) and is appended directly to the card between the full-bleed thumb and the padded `.arc-card-body` (js/views.js:2459-2464). The governing card box `.arcs .arc-card` (components.css:1822) sets `overflow:hidden` and **no padding** (padding lives on `.arc-card-body`), so "Illustrated example" renders flush against the card's left edge while the title/description below are inset 18px ‚Äî a visible alignment break unique to the illustrated example card.

### Dead weight (Arcs surface)

- **Orphan `renderArcRow` + coupled dead CSS.** `renderArcRow(arc)` (js/views.js:10925-10948, ~24 LOC) is defined once and **called nowhere** (the only other reference is a comment at 11708). It is the sole producer of `notebook-arc-row` / `notebook-arc-title` / `notebook-arc-description`, so the CSS rules `.notebook-arc-row` (components.css:4973, 4992), `.notebook-arc-title` (4999), `.notebook-arc-description` (5008), and the `:focus-visible` at 5361 are dead-by-coupling.
- **Stale legacy arcs CSS block.** With the Umber port the JS switched to `arc-card-body`/`arc-card-desc`/`arc-card-meta`/`arcs-head`/`arcs-title`/`arcs-teach`. The pre-Umber names get **0 class references in JS**: `arcs-headline`, `arcs-page-title`, `arcs-page-subtitle`, `arcs-teaching`, `arcs-create-btn`, `arc-card-text`, `arc-card-description`, `arc-card-covers`, `arc-card-cover`, `arc-card-cover-placeholder` (components.css:1518-1758), plus the dead `@media (max-width:720px)` cover-shrink rule (components.css:1764-1775) and the dead class-selector grids `.arcs-examples`/`.arcs-yours` (1586-1601).
- **Stale comment.** js/views.js:2309 asserts "The page `<h1>` already says 'Your arcs'" but the actual `<h1>` text is `'Arcs'` (js/views.js:2266).

## Arc Field / Constellation (the canvas)

**Files:** `js/arc-constellation.js` (1849 LOC), `js/tradition-forms-arc.js` (383 LOC), plus the consumers `buildArcFieldRail()` / `buildArcVoiceAffordance()` / `_arcDetailBuildSubTheoryData()` / `_stConstellationAttachInteractions()` in `js/views.js` and the constellation CSS in `assets/components.css` (~5905‚Äì6237, 8530‚Äì8687).

### What IS (verified current state)

**Two renderers; only one is wired.** `arc-constellation.js` ships two independent constellation engines. The original **book** renderer ‚Äî `renderArcConstellation()` (js/arc-constellation.js:404) with `_arcConstellationLayout`/`_arcSpareFocalLayout`/`_arcRenderQuestion`/`_arcRenderThreads`/`_arcRenderYumiLines`/`_arcRenderBooks`/`_arcRenderMarginalia`/`_arcRenderYumiCluster`/`_arcRenderLegend` ‚Äî composes books-as-tradition-glyphs with recency-faded threads, marginalia dots, a Yumi cluster, and a center question. The **sub-theory** renderer ‚Äî `renderSubTheoryConstellation()` (js/arc-constellation.js:1223) ‚Äî is the one actually mounted on `#arc/<id>` (web view, js/views.js:9878) and on Home (js/views.js:709). It renders each sub-theory as one of 16 frozen marks (`_ST_MARK_TABLE`, :870) keyed by a deterministic identity hash (`_stIdentityHash`/`_stIndices`, :526/:546), each carrying a hue body (`--subtheory-N`), a deep-stroke inner design (`--subtheory-N-edge`), a CSS-blurred hue halo, gathered-evidence dots (`_stRenderDotsForMark`, :977), and a celestial-drift wrapper.

**Drift is pure CSS, not a rAF loop.** There is no `requestAnimationFrame`/`setInterval` animation loop anywhere (`grep -c requestAnimationFrame js/arc-constellation.js` ‚Üí 0; the single `setTimeout`, :1667, is the hover-card hide delay). Drift is four `@keyframes wander{A‚ÄìD}` translate animations (components.css:6042‚Äì6055) on `.st-drift`, hash-assigned per mark via `'ABCD'.charAt(_stIdentityHash(p.id,23)%4)` (:923). Redraw cost is one full `innerHTML` rebuild per render (:1300); layer-visibility toggles flip root attributes in place with no re-render (:1306‚Äì1308, faded via CSS opacity transitions at components.css:6017‚Äì6027).

**Reduced-motion is handled ‚Äî for the canvas.** `@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)` kills the drift animation and the layer-fade transitions (components.css:6057‚Äì6067) and the hover-card fade (:6190‚Äì6192). The drift CSS is correctly scoped under `.arc-detail-web-view`, so the Home embed wrapper is inert (`.home-preview-embed` never animates).

**Chips + legend (canon H restyle-only, honored).** Connect / Reset / Layers live in a bottom control bar (`.st-control-bar-bottom`, js/views.js:9743) styled as quiet chips (components.css:5926‚Äì5936). **Layers was NOT rebuilt into toggle switches** ‚Äî it remains a popover of plain buttons (Books / Marginalia / Faint links / Muted palette, js/views.js:9826‚Äì9851), and the legend's item set (resonance / faint / gathered / incorporated / book + an interaction hint) is preserved (`_stRenderLegend`, :1117). Connect arms a pick-two link mode (`handleConnectClick`, :1732) with Esc-to-cancel (`_stConnectKeydown`, :1347); Reset nulls every placement in the arc (js/views.js:9762).

**Drag + connect + hover-card.** `attachSubTheoryDrag` (:1354) implements pointer-capture drag with a 4px tap/drag threshold (`_ST_DRAG_THRESHOLD`, :1336), a capture-phase click-swallow so a drag never also navigates (:1473), and a rich hover card (Open / Change mark / Unlink / Delete) built with `textContent` only ‚Äî user headers/quotes are never `innerHTML`'d (an XSS-safe surface, :1528). Book squares are explicitly inert (excluded from drag/connect by `data-st-book-id` bails at :1407 and :1735).

**Keyboard path exists.** `_arcMakeFocusable` (js/views.js:9324) sets `tabindex=0` + `role=button` + `aria-label` on every shape and mark `<g>` and re-fires the click on Enter/Space, and the interaction layer applies it to sub-theory shapes and marks (js/views.js:9013‚Äì9019). There is **no non-SVG fallback** (no list-equivalent inside the canvas), but the List view at the same route IS a complete non-canvas equivalent of the data.

### Regressions / divergences

**Light-on-light contrast failure on the dark `#arc` route (the most serious issue).** The `#arc` route is dark-grounded ‚Äî `umberGroundDark` includes `arc` (js/views.js:369), so `body[data-ground="dark"]` remaps `--ink`‚Üí`--text-d` (#f0e3c8) and `--ink-2/3/4`‚Üí`--muted` (#c2a87f) (theme.css:336‚Äì344). But the sub-theory SVG paints its OWN opaque **bright goldenrod** ground (`fill="url(#tfa-stage)"`, stops #fbf2da‚Üí#d8bd80, tradition-forms-arc.js:73‚Äì77) as a full-bleed rect (js/arc-constellation.js:1268), and `.arc-detail-web-view::before` was deliberately blanked (`background-image:none`, components.css:5998) "because the field is now-DARK." The result: the question label (`fill="var(--ink-2)"`, :853), legend text (`var(--ink-2,#633806)`, :1129), Yumi label/circle (`var(--ink,#412402)`, :1106‚Äì1107), and empty-state prompt (:862) all resolve to light tan/cream on the bright goldenrod ground ‚Äî measured **1.25‚Äì2.04** for the inks and **1.14** for the Yumi `--ink`, far below AA 4.5 and even below the 3.0 UI floor. The `#633806` literal in `var(--token, #633806)` would give 7.17 on this ground, but the CSS variable always wins so the fallback never applies. This is a dual-ground port regression: the SVG ground stayed bright while the tokens flipped dark. (Contrast computed with WCAG 2.1 relative-luminance.)

**The styled keyboard focus ring never matches the live marks.** The focus-visible ring (components.css:6222‚Äì6237) targets only the **book** renderer's attributes ‚Äî `[data-book-id]`, `[data-thread-a]`, `[data-marginalia-book-id]`, `[data-yumi-cluster]`, `[data-question]` ‚Äî none of which the arc-detail web view ever emits (it runs the sub-theory renderer, whose marks carry `data-st-sub-id`/`data-st-mark`). Confirmed: `grep` for any `:focus`/`outline` rule mentioning `data-st-sub-id`/`data-st-mark` in components.css returns nothing, while the `[data-book-id]:focus-visible` control matches at 6230. So tabbing reaches sub-theory marks (they have `tabindex=0`) but shows only the browser's default UA outline (and the `outline:none` reset at 6222‚Äì6228 doesn't even cover them) ‚Äî an a11y focus-visibility gap on the one keyboard path the canvas offers.

### Dead weight

**The entire book renderer is dead (~412 LOC).** `renderArcConstellation` has zero call sites outside its own definition/comments (`grep` confirms only views.js:8605 mentions it, in a comment). Its layout/render helpers (lines 56‚Äì467) are all unreachable, as are its views.js companions: `_arcDetailBuildConstellationData` (js/views.js:8615, never called ‚Äî only the def + 2 comments) and `_arcConstellationAttachInteractions` (js/views.js:8832 comment notes it as a sibling; the live route never invokes it). The matching focus-ring CSS block (components.css:6222‚Äì6237) is therefore also dead chrome.

**Emitted-but-unconsumed SVG defs every render.** `_stGetDefs()` (:588) is still called on every sub-theory render (:1267) and serializes a `st-grain` pattern + 16 `st-halo-1..16` radial gradients (:590‚Äì603) ‚Äî but the live mark recipe uses `url(#tfa-shine)` (:954) + an inline blur, never `url(#st-halo)` or `url(#st-grain)`. Confirmed: `grep st-halo|st-grain` finds only the definitions and a self-admitting comment ("remain as dead code (removal is a later cleanup)", :897). 17 dead defs are written into the DOM on each render.

**Three superseded mark helpers.** `_stSilhouette` (:614), `_stTreatment` (:649, ~120 LOC of 14 motifs), and `_stRenderMarks` (:1021) have no call sites (the 16-mark table + `_stRenderDotsForMark` replaced them). `shapeLines` (js/views.js:8906) is built but its binding was intentionally dropped (:9003). The back-compat shim `_stIdentity` (:571) survives only because the builder still stores `shapeKey`/`color` the renderer ignores.

### Token / convention drift

**Hardcoded hex in the renderer.** Three bare hexes violate the CSS-vars-only rule: `#2A2018` (st-grain stroke, :591 ‚Äî but this is in a dead def), `#966E28` (resonance + faint **edge color**, used live at :1076/:1092‚Äì1094, on the actually-drawn edges), and `#FFF8E7` (cream, muted-body radial :937 and the preview-defs :1845). `tradition-forms-arc.js` carries 100 hex literals (the whole tradition palette) ‚Äî a known pre-token design artifact, only relevant if the dead book renderer is ever revived. The grain/halo defs and `tfa-stage`/`tfa-qhalo`/`tfa-shine` are likewise literal-stop'd by design (shared-def `currentColor` is a documented Chrome black-trap).

### Performance note
Each `renderArcDetail` rebuild calls `renderSubTheoryConstellation` (full `innerHTML` swap) then `_stConstellationAttachInteractions` + `attachSubTheoryDrag`, re-querying and re-binding listeners on the fresh DOM (listeners GC with the discarded SVG ‚Äî no teardown, no leak). With the dead `_stGetDefs` output, every render also serializes 17 unused gradient/pattern defs. For typical arc sizes (‚â§ a handful of sub-theories) this is negligible; it is not a hot loop (no rAF), so the cost is bounded to user-triggered re-renders.

## Arc Interior + Sub-theory Page

Scope: `renderArcDetail()` (views.js:9477, dark ground), `renderSubTheoryPage()` (:7467, bright ground), `renderSubTheoryReadOnly()` (:7285), `openSymbolPicker()` (:6802), `openArcDeleteConfirm()` (:10040), `openArcEditor()` (:2143), the new-subtheory route (:482), the arc-voice affordance (:9398), the arc-field rail (:9423), and the Web-view constellation interaction layer (`attachSubTheoryDrag`, the hover card) in arc-constellation.js. The data layer is `createSubTheory`/`updateSubTheory`/`addEvidence`/`setSubTheoryPosition`/`linkSubTheories` (state.js:1724‚Äì1959, 1991).

### What is verified present (IS)

**Create / compose path.** The hash `arc/<arcId>/new-subtheory` (views.js:482) mints a draft via `createSubTheory` and `location.replace`s to `#subtheory/<id>` ‚Äî `replace` (not assign) keeps the create-hash out of history so Back cannot re-mint a second empty draft (:477). `createSubTheory` (state.js:1730) guards on a real parent arc (`state.arcs[arcId]`), stamps `userId` from the creator, and self-persists. A header is optional (empty string accepted), consistent with the gather‚Üísub-theory paths (:1173). The new-subtheory affordance is rendered in three places: the header `+ Sub-theory` button (List view only, suppressed in Web ‚Äî :9598), the Web bottom control bar (built but deliberately unappended ‚Äî :9865), and the arc-field rail `+ Add a sub-theory` (:9461).

**Register / Write|Preview / Published controls.** The sub-theory page (:7467) carries a segmented PUBLIC|INTELLECTUAL register toggle (:7575), a per-register Write|Preview pill (:7648), and a separate "Published" toggle (:7720) that swaps the editor for `renderSubTheoryReadOnly(state.subTheories[id], 'published')`. All three text fields blur-save through `updateSubTheory` (:7547, 7586, 7594). `applyEditorView()` (:7664) is the single source of truth for which surface shows. Maturity is a live computed band (`_stComputeMaturity`, views.js:8754 = `(pubLen + intelLen + 80*evCount) / 1500`, clamped 0‚Äì1) rendered as nascent/developing/established with a glow whose opacity tracks the value (:7556‚Äì7565).

**Inline cite-weave.** The asterisk convention is parsed by the pure `parseCitations` (:7211) and surfaced through `renderCitationPreview` (:8030): matched titles get a `.subtheory-cite` dot, unmatched italics render `<em>`, a coach line teaches the convention until a citation resolves (:8067). There is a Cite-from-the-rail insert at the last-focused caret (`insertCitationAtCursor`, :7608), a `*`-triggered autocomplete of attached titles (:7985), a hover card (:7823, body-mounted `.arc-tooltip`, textContent-only), and a right-click/long-press disambiguation chooser whose choice persists to `subTheory.citationPins` (:7904, keyed by lowercased phrase, routed in both the editor and the read-only render). All preview painting is `textContent`/`createElement` only ‚Äî no innerHTML with body text (XSS-safe).

**Evidence rail (Checkpoint C).** The rail (:8096) lists Attached evidence (hollow teal "gathered" rings, :8193), a From-this-arc source picker (books from `arc.bookIds`, non-private entries from `arc.entryIds`; private entries skipped per principle #5, :8392), an inline quote+annotation attach editor (:8286), and an external-source form with a required-title gate (:8454). Attaching routes through `addEvidence` (state.js:1991) and repaints in place via `refreshAttached` (:8264) ‚Äî never a full re-render, protecting un-blurred prose. The rail collapses to a mobile bottom sheet ‚â§720px with backdrop + Escape dismiss (:8116). Private/missing entries are tagged "private ‚Äî excluded when published" in the editing rail (:8225) and silently dropped in the published render (:7310).

**Unlink / delete affordances.** Delete is reachable on the sub-theory page (`stDeleteBtn`, :7532, routes to parent arc on confirm) and in the Web hover card (arc-constellation.js:1602). Unlink lives ONLY in the Web hover card (:1580) ‚Äî shown when the sub has ‚â•1 edge ‚Äî handing off to `confirmUnlinkSubTheory` (views.js:7103), a per-connection modal (never a bulk wipe) reusing `unlinkSubTheories`. `deleteSubTheory` cascades edge removal over a snapshot (state.js:1805).

**Arc voice (Stage C).** `buildArcVoiceAffordance` (:9398) mounts a quiet "Ask Yumi what she sees here" button inline under the view toggle, signed-in only. `requestArcVoice` (:9368) calls `YumiBrain.considerArcVoice` (yumi-brain.js:2351), which gates consent‚Üíbudget‚Üícontext‚Üíweb-angle‚Üígenerate‚Üígrade; every LLM link is `_yumiWithTimeout`-wrapped with a rejection‚Üífallback handler (gen at 2340, grade at 746, web at 1384), so the chain always resolves and the button re-enables. A non-PASS renders the fixed `ARC_VOICE_FALLBACK` (solicited, never silence). All inline styles are token-based (`var(--gold)`, `var(--surface-2)`, etc.).

**Symbol picker.** `openSymbolPicker` (:6802) is a full shape√ócolor override dialog (16 shapes, 16 hues, Auto/Reset-to-id-hash), persisting `markShape`/`markColor` (clamped 0‚Äì15). The `markChip` on the sub-theory head (:7510) is a live mini-render that opens it; Change-mark in the hover card hands off via the `window.openSymbolPicker` hook.

**Ground.** Arc detail renders dark (`umberGroundDark[arc]=1`, views.js:369), sub-theory bright (not in the map ‚Üí bright). The sub-theory page uses single-valued bright tokens (`--page-2`, `--line-page`, `--meta`, `--teal`, `--gold-ink`) ‚Äî all defined in theme.css.

### Regressions / divergences

- **Arc-detail List render crashes on an arc missing `entryIds`/`bookIds`.** Lines 9924 and 9934 read `arc.bookIds.length`/`arc.entryIds.length` **unguarded**, while the SAME function guards the sub-meta line (`arc.bookIds && arc.bookIds.length`, :9572), the rail (`Array.isArray(arc.bookIds)`, :8376/8386), and both constellation adapters (:8618, 8733). No `ensureArcFields` helper exists anywhere (grep: 0 hits); arcs are splat-only on Firestore merge with no backfill, and migrate() never runs on the merge path. A remote/legacy/console arc without `entryIds` throws `TypeError: Cannot read properties of undefined (reading 'length')`, aborting the whole arc-detail render ‚Äî the same defensive-gap class that produced the v3.143 account white-screen.

- **Sub-theory publish is dead.** `status` and `publishedAt` exist in the schema (createSubTheory :1747‚Äì1749) and are validated by `ensureSubTheoryFields` (state.js:660), but `status: 'published'` is NEVER set anywhere (grep for the literal: 0 hits) and nothing reads `status === 'published'` (every `.status` in views.js refers to BOOK read-status). The "Published" toggle is a preview render only; there is no publish action and no way for a sub-theory to leave `'draft'`. `updateSubTheory` explicitly refuses to touch `status`/`publishedAt` (:1762). The register/publish "controls" are therefore preview affordances, not a publish lifecycle.

- **Intellectual register is write-only.** `bodyIntellectual` is editable (:7590), feeds maturity (:8756), spotlight search (spotlight.js:63), and the row-label fallback (:10539), but is surfaced in NO read view: `renderSubTheoryReadOnly` renders only `bodyPublic` (:7374). A reader (and the published preview) never sees the intellectual register the author wrote.

- **Unlink is desktop-Web-only.** The unlink affordance ‚Äî the named smoke-test requirement ‚Äî lives solely in the constellation hover card, which is bound `if (!isTouch)` (arc-constellation.js:1672; touch has no hover, tap navigates). On touch there is no unlink path at all, and unlink is absent from List view and from the sub-theory page itself. Change-mark has the same touch gap (page markChip is its only touch fallback); Delete is the only per-sub action reachable on every surface.

### COULD-level observations
Captured separately. Highlights: add `ensureArcFields`/guards to close the List crash; wire a real publish lifecycle or remove the dead `status` field + relabel the "Published" toggle; surface the intellectual register in a read view or gate it as private-by-design; give unlink a non-hover home (List view per-edge control or a connections list on the sub-theory page); add a rejection handler to `requestArcVoice`'s `.then`; drop the dead `_arcDetailBuildConstellationData`.

## Book Detail + Artifact

Surface entry points (all verified): `renderBookDetail()` js/views.js:5963, `renderArtifact()` js/views.js:8538, `openMarginaliaEditor()` js/views.js:10148, `openArtifactEditor()` js/views.js:10221, `openBookArcPicker()` js/views.js:10340, `openBookSendToSubTheory()` js/views.js:10622, `buildBookshopUrl()` js/views.js:242, `buildSelfHealingCover()` js/views.js:5098. Both surfaces are tagged `data-ground=bright` (renderRoute js/views.js:369-371; neither `book` nor `artifact` is in `umberGroundDark`), matching the spec.

### What IS (verified)

**Renderer markup.** `renderBookDetail` builds a `.bd-grid` `<header>` (js/views.js:5990) with two cells: `.bd-cover-col` (cover + `.bd-actions`) and `.bd-content` (title/author/meta/biblio/status/desc/lenses/rating/artifact-card). Action order inside `.bd-actions` matches canon ¬ß4-I: primary `btn btn-primary` "Add to arc‚Ä¶" (js/views.js:6279), then a `.row2` secondary pair [Send-to-sub-theory | Add Marginalia] (js/views.js:6302-6306), then the status-branch button, then themes, then the danger Remove. The six-branch (status √ó hasArtifact) matrix is explicit and standalone (js/views.js:6325-6386); branches 4/5/6 render "Open Artifact" `<a href="#artifact/‚Ä¶">`.

**Self-healing cover (solid).** `buildSelfHealingCover` (js/views.js:5098) walks `book.coverCandidates` (or `[coverUrl]`) on each `error`, falls to a typographic "cover pending" placeholder when exhausted, and maintains a `coverBrokenIds` registry that clears on `load` (js/views.js:5108-5121). Candidates are populated by the resolver (integrations.js:1737); review-confirm book records carry an `id` field (js/views.js:5424) so the registry key is sound.

**Picker `scrollIntoView` (shipped, verified not rebuilt).** Both `openBookArcPicker` (js/views.js:10368-10370) and `openBookSendToSubTheory` (js/views.js:10632-10634) call `host.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'nearest'})` after mounting. The arc picker re-opens in place with an "Already in that arc." note on a duplicate (js/views.js:10357); the sub-theory picker supports multi-attach with per-row checkmarks and a toast (js/views.js:10585-10602).

**Marginalia = the WritingCanvas adopter (verified).** `openMarginaliaEditor` is the ONLY book-detail editor wired to `createWritingCanvas` (js/views.js:10156), with `surfaceId:'marginalia'`, focus mode, autosave (700ms debounce + blur flush, writing-canvas.js:521-532), markdown undo stack, and a quiet `.wc-done` exit. Saved marginalia cards re-render through the SAME renderer (`wcRenderMarkdown`, writing-canvas.js:36) in `renderNotebookEntry` (js/views.js:10705-10707), closing the editor/card split. The canvas/`.wc-*` CSS is complete and token-clean (components.css:10539-10583).

**Artifact (finished-room) path.** First-finish is ceremonial: the `reading && !artifact` "I've finished this" button stamps `status='read'`+`finishedAt` and chains `openArtifactEditor` (js/views.js:6336-6344). `openArtifactEditor` (js/views.js:10221) writes through `ensureOneArtifact` (state.js:961, no-op on second call ‚Äî constitutional #3). `renderArtifact` (js/views.js:8538) paints title + `white-space:pre-wrap` body + a substrate link back, with defensive not-found/empty states for hand-typed hashes.

### Regressions / divergence

**Mobile reorder (canon ¬ß4-I) is DEAD ‚Äî class-name drift.** The ¬ß4-I single-column block (components.css:5528-5566) targets the OLD names `.book-detail-header`/`-cover-col`/`-content`/`-title`/`-author`/`-meta`/`-actions`/`-artifact-card`/`-actions-row`, but the Umber-port renderer emits `.bd-grid`/`.bd-cover-col`/`.bd-content`/`.bd-title`/`.bd-author`/`.bd-meta`/`.bd-actions`/`.bd-artifact`/`.row2`. None of the layout selectors match. The base `.bd-grid` rule (`grid-template-columns:260px 1fr`, components.css:2991) has NO media query, so it applies at 390px too ‚Äî leaving ~110px for the content column. The mobile cover cap (`max-width:200px`) and the side-by-side secondary pair also never apply. The CSS comment at components.css:2986 even admits "the live `.book-detail-*` rules for the mapped classes are now dead" ‚Äî the mobile block is part of that dead set and was never migrated. (Only `.book-detail-quote` and `.find-this-book` still emit, but their `order` is inert because their parent is the un-dissolved `.bd-grid`.) [requires live verification of the 390px collapse.]

**`.book-detail` padding/width double-rule.** Two `.book-detail` rules exist: components.css:2551 (`max-width:1080px; padding:48px 32px`) and the later Umber rule components.css:2990 (`max-width:1000px; padding:0 var(--sp-5)`). The later wins, so the page loses its 48px top padding (top/bottom become 0) and the width steps to 1000px. [requires live verification of top breathing room.]

**Artifact surface UNADOPTED (substrate inconsistency).** Marginalia uses WritingCanvas + live markdown; the Artifact editor (`openArtifactEditor`‚Üí`openEditor`, js/views.js:2002) is the OLD plain `<textarea>`, and `renderArtifact` shows the body as `textContent`/`pre-wrap` (js/views.js:8591) ‚Äî no markdown render. The two writing surfaces on the same book diverge in capability and look.

**Marginalia is write-once (no edit affordance).** `openMarginaliaEditor` is hardcoded to a new entry (`initialValue:''`, `entryId=null`, js/views.js:10154-10159); the saved card's action row (js/views.js:10730-10850) offers gather/add-to-arc/file/send-to-sub/**delete** but NO edit. A typo in saved marginalia can only be fixed by deleting and re-writing.

**Meta-count vs list predicate mismatch.** The `.bd-meta` marginalia count (js/views.js:6060-6071) filters only `register==='marginalia'` + `bookIds.indexOf(bookId)`, with NO `userId` guard, whereas the rendered marginalia list (js/views.js:6726-6733) additionally requires `e.userId===user.uid`. Per-uid state bucketing masks this today, but the two predicates can diverge.

### Data durability (CRITICAL)

**Book Artifacts are localStorage-only ‚Äî no Firestore sync.** `grep -c bookArtifacts js/integrations.js` = 0: the onAuthStateChanged merge syncs books/arcs/subTheories/userThemes/notebookEntries but never `state.bookArtifacts`. `openArtifactEditor`'s onSave calls `saveState()` with no `markBooksDirty`/artifact-dirty flag (js/views.js:10242), and there is no artifact dirty flag or cloud-save branch anywhere (state.js:759 comment is stale ‚Äî it predates the arcs/notebook sync that later landed). The Artifact ‚Äî the ceremonial "written once, yours" object whose own card copy promises permanence (js/views.js:6229) ‚Äî is therefore never written to the cloud and is absent on any new device, fresh install, or after a localStorage clear.

### Mobile / a11y

- `.bd-meta` 11px mono in `--meta` (#9a7e4e on bright ‚âà 3.4:1, components.css:2999) and `.find-this-book` 12px mono in `--ink-3` (components.css:1864) both fail WCAG AA for small text.
- `.wc-done` ‚Äî the marginalia editor's only exit affordance ‚Äî is 11px uppercase mono in `--meta` (components.css:10577), sub-AA.
- `body.wc-focus` is added on editor focus and removed only on blur/destroy (writing-canvas.js:566-567); a programmatic hash change while the editor holds focus (e.g. browser back) can leave `.app-nav` dimmed. [requires live verification.]

## Account / Reader-Portrait (dark ground)

Entry: `renderAccountPage()` (js/views.js:13167), `buildReaderModelSection(uid)` (js/views.js:11935), `openAccountDeleteConfirm(uid)` (js/views.js:11459). The whole page is built on a single detached `wrap` `<section>` and attached to the DOM exactly once, at the very end (`host.appendChild(wrap)` js/views.js:14211). The page is forced to `data-ground="dark"` (js/views.js:369-371, `account` in `umberGroundDark`).

### IS ‚Äî verified current state

**Render architecture.** `renderAccountPage` builds, in order on the detached `wrap`: signed-out early-return (13183-13207); HERO card with gradient monogram + wired ‚úé pencils (13176-13290); a bare STANCE covenant line (13294-13300); **VALUES** "place a stone" editor (13312-13413); the hidden profile edit form (13419-13490); STAT CARDS + an empty `account-expand-host` (13497-13518); **REVEALED-SELF** (segmented View-by toggle, categorize-as-dialogue, FIELD, GALAXY, RETURNS, consent-gated THREADS) (13524-13889); **JOURNEY** (13895-13918); **CAPSTONE EMBLEM** (13923-14019); TRANSPARENCY card (14031-14095); the reader-model section (14102); the "your data" card with Export/Sign-out (14104-14173); an actions card (14176-14179); the danger/delete card (14181-14209).

**The v3.142 crash class is contained, not merely patched.** The audited risk ‚Äî `document.getElementById` on a node still inside the detached `wrap` subtree ‚Äî does NOT recur anywhere else in this render path. The only `getElementById` between 13167 and 14212 is js/views.js:13168 (`document.getElementById(APP_EL_ID)`, the app root, already in the document); the only other hit in that range is a code comment at js/views.js:13964. The capstone correctly queries the detached card via `capCard.querySelector('#account-portrait-...')` (js/views.js:13968-13973) with each `addEventListener` null-guarded (js/views.js:3988-14018). `buildReaderModelSection` (11935-12443) contains **zero** `getElementById`/`document.querySelector` calls ‚Äî it wires handlers to nodes it just created and re-renders coarsely via `renderAccountPage()`. The deferred-binding lookups that DO use `document.querySelector` (`_accountHostReset` js/views.js:11599-11601, `_accountToggleCategory` js/views.js:11606-11607) run only on user click, after attachment ‚Äî safe.

**Crash-isolation umbrellas.** Four portrait sections are individually wrapped in ES3 `try/catch` (VALUES 13312/13413, REVEALED-SELF 13524/13889, JOURNEY 13895/13918, CAPSTONE 13923/14019), each degrading to "section absent" with `console.error`. This is the correct hardening pattern post-v3.143.

**Reader-model CRUD + consent (js/views.js:11935-12443).** Five toggles share one write path (`setProfile` ‚Üí `saveProfileToFirestore`, fire-and-forget, then `renderAccountPage()` re-render): reader-model opt-in `yumiReaderModel` (flipConsent 11953), web-grounding `yumiWebGrounding` (flipWebConsent 11962), voice `voiceOn` (flipVoiceOn 11971), talk-mode (flipTalkMode 11979); a sixth, the same `yumiReaderModel` flag, is ALSO flipped from the portrait THREADS card (js/views.js:13861-13864) ‚Äî two independent controls write the same consent bit. Threads list supports edit (gated on `active` = opt-in AND `yumiReadsAlong`) and delete (always available); arc-prose block routes through the content-aware `readerProfileSource` resolver (js/views.js:12362) so a hand-edit is not overwritten by Yumi's auto-read. "Forget everything" (`clearReaderModel` 12423) is shown only when data exists, available even when consent is off ‚Äî correct "reader owns their data" posture. Opening the panel with consent on fires `YumiBrain.considerProfileRefresh` (js/views.js:12437), self-gated, which can trigger a second full `renderAccountPage()` on a successful write.

**Reader-portrait blocks read live state, escaped.** Every user-controlled string injected via `innerHTML` is run through `_portraitEsc` (js/views.js:12461): RETURNS titles/authors (12965/12979/12982), JOURNEY book/lens/sub titles (13121/13145/13157), the dialogue proposed/confirmed names (13589/13594), galaxy/field column labels (12631/12655/12812/12858). The VALUES "stones" use `document.createTextNode` (js/views.js:13355). No XSS surface found on this page. The book-mark glyphs in the stat-panel sub-theory rows use the id-hash path `stHashIndices` + `_stPickerMarkSvg` (js/views.js:11670-11678), honoring `markShape`/`markColor` with a hash default ‚Äî consistent with the locked DECOUPLE decision.

**Delete-account flow (js/views.js:11459 ‚Üí js/integrations.js:887).** `deleteAccount` deletes 7 Firestore docs, then wipes local, then attempts auth-record deletion; `requires-recent-login` (and any auth error) is handled gracefully as `deleted-data-only` (integrations.js:920-929) ‚Äî data is already gone, so it signs out and surfaces a soft note rather than resurrecting. A hard Firestore-delete error aborts before any local wipe with `{status:'error'}` (integrations.js:932-942), and the confirm UI restores the button and shows a "Nothing was removed" note (js/views.js:11486-11494). On success it `location.reload()`s.

### REGRESSIONS / DIVERGENCE

- **Export omits reader-owned data built ON THIS PAGE.** `exportWorkspace` (js/state.js:1500-1528) ‚Äî the data behind the "Export to JSON" button (js/views.js:14143-14162) ‚Äî returns only `profile, books, arcs, subTheories, notebookEntries`. It does NOT include `userThemes` (lenses, which this page's categorize-as-dialogue creates via `createUserTheme`), the reader-model (`state.users[uid].readerModel` threads + arc-prose, a sibling of `profile`, not inside it), or `bookArtifacts`. The "your data ‚Ä¶ take a copy" covenant (js/views.js:14115-14117) is therefore incomplete for exactly the artifacts this surface produces.
- **Export leaks non-owned records.** The same function exports the FULL global `state.arcs`, `state.subTheories`, and `state.notebookEntries` maps unfiltered (js/state.js:1524-1526) ‚Äî it does not filter by `userId === uid`, so a user's "copy of my data" includes seed records and any other-user records present in memory. (Books ARE correctly uid-filtered at 1507-1518.)
- **Reader-model section is the one unguarded tail builder.** `wrap.appendChild(buildReaderModelSection(uid))` (js/views.js:14102) sits OUTSIDE any try/catch, before the "your data", actions, and danger/delete cards. A throw inside it would abort the rest of the render and leave the user with no Export / Sign-out / Delete affordance ‚Äî a milder echo of the v3.142 failure mode the portrait umbrellas were added to prevent.

### Contrast (dark ground)

The page renders at `data-ground="dark"` and uses `--teal` (4√ó), `--journal-color` (1√ó), and `--danger` (3√ó) in the account block. Per the foundation token audit these resolve sub-AA on the dark surface (teal #2e8a93 ‚âà 3.41, journal #7d6db0 ‚âà 3.09, river/question #3a5a8a ‚âà 1.98). These appear in portrait accent text/marks and the danger affordance; meta/hint lines (`--ink-3`/`--ink-4` family, the `.hint` eyebrow tails) are the readability risk on body-adjacent copy. [contrast values inherited from foundation pass; live computed-style check warranted.]

## About surface (`#about` -> `renderAbout()`)

**Route & ground.** `#about` is wired in `renderRoute` at `js/views.js:556-563` (clears the three open-pointers, `saveState()`, `renderAbout()`), with `activeRoute='about'` set at `js/views.js:397-399` and a top-nav link at `index.html:29` (`<a href="#about" data-route="about">About</a>`). It is correctly a **bright-ground** surface: `umberGroundDark` (`js/views.js:369`) lists only `{home,books,arcs,arc,account}`, so About falls through to `data-ground="bright"`. It is also a valid Yumi nav target (`ROUTER_NAV_TARGETS`, `js/yumi-brain.js:2557`). The renderer (`js/views.js:14222-14462`) is a single `innerHTML` build of a static orientation page: hero + a segmented switcher between two panels ‚Äî Panel 1 "What Praxis is" (four explainer sections 01-04, each with lexicon entries and three SVG infographics: banking‚Üîproblem-posing `#bp`, the `.triad`, and the reflection-action loop `.ra`) and Panel 2 "Re-enter a page" (four native `<details>` accordions). It contains **no `<a href>` links** (grep over `14222-14462` returned zero hrefs) ‚Äî so there are no dead links, and the only navigation off the page is the global nav.

### IS ‚Äî verified current state
- **Renders entirely from token-driven CSS, no raw hex.** The full `.about` block (`assets/components.css:9466-9695`) has **0 raw hex** (`grep '#[0-9a-fA-F]{3,6}'` over the block = 0); the one `color-mix(in srgb, var(--gold) 55%, transparent)` (`:9509`) is token-derived. Surfaces use `--surface`/`--surface-2`/`--glass-2`, inks `--ink`/`--ink-2`/`--ink-3`/`--ink-4`/`--gold-text`, radii `--radius-*`, shadows `--shadow-1`/`--shadow-2`, and a locally-scoped `--font-script` CJK/Greek fallback (`:9467`) so `Áî±Áæé`/`œÄœÅ·æ∂ŒæŒπœÇ` never tofu.
- **ES3-clean.** The four handlers (`renderAbout`, `aboutWireBp` `:14466`, `aboutShowPanel` `:14483`, `aboutWireSeg` `:14503`) use `var`/`function` only ‚Äî no `const`/`let`/arrow/class/template-literal/`.catch`/`.finally` (verified by reading `14222-14507`).
- **Switcher is styled and functional.** The HTML emits `.seg`/`.seg-opt`/`.is-on` (`:14238-14240`); the Umber-port appendix defines `.about .seg` / `.seg-opt` / `.seg-opt.is-on` (`:9684-9686`, gradient pill via `--grad` + `--text-on-dark`). `aboutWireSeg` toggles `.is-active` on `.about-panel` (`:9642-9643`) and `.is-on` on the buttons.
- **Glyph crests reuse the one shared component.** `[data-yumi-glyph]` placeholders are filled by `yumiGlyphNode(size)` (`js/views.js:14434-14440`; defined `js/yumi-ui.js:143`), the single static-Yumi mark ‚Äî no second sprite.
- **Mobile treatment is minimal but present.** Inside the About block there is exactly one `@media (max-width:759px)` (`:9576-9577`) collapsing `.yumi-contrast` 2-col‚Üí1-col, plus two `prefers-reduced-motion` blocks (`:9631-9634` SVG/spin off; `:9665-9669` panel-fade/accordion off). All other responsiveness is `clamp()` type-scaling + `flex-wrap`; the SVG infographics scale via `width:100%;height:auto` (`:9594`, `:9615`).

### REGRESSIONS / DIVERGENCE
- **Large dead-CSS residue from the Umber port.** The June 2026 Umber port appended a new frame (`:9671-9695`, renamed root to `.about`, native `<details>`, `.seg` pill, per-entry lexicon cards) but **never removed the superseded pre-port rules**. ~38 declaration lines now style classes the current `renderAbout` no longer emits: `.about-eyebrow` (`:9476`), `.about-lede-hero` (`:9496`), `.about-hero-mark` (`:9508`), `.hairline-gold` (`:9509`), `.about-hero-rule` (`:9510`), `.about-seg-wrap` (`:9637`), `.about-seg-btn` √ó3 (`:9639-9641`), and the entire re-arm accordion family `.rearm-head/.rearm-eyebrow/.rearm-h2/.rearm-sub/.rearm-list/.rearm-card*/.rearm-card-head/.rearm-card-label/.rearm-card-teaser/.rearm-chevron/.rearm-card-body/.rearm-card-inner/.rearm-yumi-line` (`:9647-9663`). Verified each is rendered 0√ó by JS (`14222-14462`) yet present in CSS. The hero now uses the **global** `.eyebrow` (`:804`) and `.about-lede` instead of the orphaned `.about-eyebrow`/`.about-lede-hero`.
- **Duplicate `.about-seg` rule.** Defined twice: `:9638` (`inline-flex`, `margin:34px auto 0`, `--wash` pill bg, border) and `:9683` (`flex; justify-content:center; margin:var(--sp-5) 0`). The later wins, but the first carries a now-unused pill background/border that no longer matches the markup (the pill moved to the inner `.seg`).
- **Hero-glyph size override.** Markup requests a 56px crest (`data-yumi-glyph="56"`, `:14234`) and `yumiGlyph` writes `width="56" height="56"` onto the SVG (`js/yumi-ui.js:102-103`), but `.about .about-mark svg { width:60px; height:60px }` (`:9681`) overrides it to 60px. Intent vs. rendered size diverge by 4px.

### ACCESSIBILITY
- **Tablist/toggle ARIA mismatch.** The switcher container is `role="tablist"` (`:14238`) but its children are `<button aria-pressed=...>` (toggle-button semantics), not `role="tab"`/`aria-selected` (`:14239-14240`), and the two panels are plain `<section data-panel>` with **no** `role="tabpanel"` / `aria-labelledby` (`:14245`, `:14417`). A screen reader announces a tablist whose members aren't tabs and whose panels aren't associated. Keyboard operation itself is fine (native `<button type="button">`, focusable, Enter/Space).
- **Sub-AA secondary text.** Per the foundation contrast pass, `--ink-3`/`--ink-4` ‚âà #9a7e4e ‚âà 3.41-3.56:1 on the bright page ‚Äî passes 3:1 (large/non-essential) but fails 4.5:1 (normal body). On About these are almost all small mono labels/eyebrows/captions/glosses (`.about-figcap` `:9582`, `.lex-pron` `:9533`, `.ideo-en` `:9562`, `.triad-gloss` `:9627`), which is defensible. The one normal-size body case is `.lex-pos` (serif italic ~1.02rem, `--ink-3`, `:9534`).

## Yumi Panel (Bloom FAB + Chat) + Transparency / What-Yumi-Sees

Surface scope: `js/yumi-ui.js` (1928 LOC; `wc -l js/yumi-ui.js`) for the floating panel, Bloom FAB, chat send/round-trip, onboarding state machine, voice in/out wiring, and the lens panel; the transparency builders in `js/views.js` (`buildTransparencyContent` :11132, `openTransparencyView` :11105, `renderWhatYumiSeesPage` :11303, plus the 4 `renderTransparency*` helpers :11325‚Äì11424). The brain-side chat path lives in `js/yumi-brain.js` (`sendMessage` :754, `assembleContextData` :178, `classifyUtterance` :2639). TTS playback is `playLine` in `js/integrations.js` :2039.

### IS ‚Äî verified current behavior

**Chat round-trip.** The Send button handler (`yumi-ui.js:1144`) trims input, strips the empty-state node, and dispatches through four mutually-exclusive interceptors in order: onboarding (`onb.active`, :1160), pending co-write weave (`YumiBrain.pendingComplicate`, :1176), pending NAME proposal (`YumiBrain.pendingNotice`, :1196), then the normal path. The normal path sets `yumi_request_in_flight=true`, disables Send, renders the typing indicator, and runs the router (`classifyUtterance`, :1265): a non-`CONVERSATION` verdict is handled read-only by `routeCommand` (NAV/OPEN, :534) and never reaches the model; `CONVERSATION` (and the router's rejection arm) falls through to `runChat()` (:1237) ‚Üí `YumiBrain.sendMessage` (`yumi-brain.js:754`). Verified: the router fail-closes to `CONVERSATION` on empty/over-budget/timeout/error (`classifyUtterance` :2641/2647/2672), and the UI's rejection arm also calls `runChat()` (:1275), so a reader's message is never silently dropped.

**Graceful endpoint failure (verified static).** `sendMessage` throws `'proxy <status>: <body>'` on a non-OK response (`yumi-brain.js:775-778`). `runChat`'s `.catch` (`yumi-ui.js:1249`) logs, calls `removeTypingIndicator()`, and `renderError()` with the default copy `'Something went wrong reaching Yumi. Try again.'` (`yumi-ui.js:288`); `.finally` (:1254) clears `yumi_request_in_flight` and re-enables Send. So a gated/down proxy surfaces the expected message, not a crash. A *gate*-suppressed reply (gradeUtterance fail-closed) returns `{silent:true}` (`yumi-brain.js:800`) and `runChat` renders nothing (:1242) ‚Äî intentional silence, no chrome.

**Fail-closed gate.** `gradeUtterance` is wrapped in `_yumiWithTimeout` (`yumi-brain.js:746`, 12 s) and fail-closes to `{pass:false}` on every error path. `sendMessage` awaits it (:797) before appending the assistant turn ‚Äî a suppressed reply is never written to memory and so never appears in the transparency "Recent turns" section.

**Transparency single-source.** `buildTransparencyContent(snap, context)` (`views.js:11132`) is the ONE builder; both the Notebook panel (`openTransparencyView` :11105) and the routed `#yumi-sees` page (`renderWhatYumiSeesPage` :11303) feed it a FRESH `window.YumiBrain.getContextSnapshot()` ‚Äî which is an alias of `assembleContextData` (`yumi-brain.js:2748`). The in-panel "What Yumi sees" fold (`buildYumiPanel` :1075-1091) renders the SAME builder over the conversation (body `display:none`, conversation preserved), falling back to `location.hash='yumi-sees'` if the builder/snapshot is unavailable (:1076). Every dynamic value goes in via `textContent`; web-derived strings in `buildGroundingChips` (`yumi-ui.js:184`) are href-validated to `http(s)` with `rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow"` and never `innerHTML`'d.

**Private-filter correctness.** The snapshot the transparency view shows is filtered identically to what Yumi receives: `assembleContextData` skips `isPrivate === true` notebook entries (`yumi-brain.js:218`) and artifacts (:266), caps to top-3 newest, truncates bodies to 200 chars (:234), and zeroes `recentEntries`/`recentArtifacts` entirely when the master `profile.yumiReadsAlong === false` (:326). The framing copy ("Entries marked private do not appear here‚Ä¶", `views.js:11166`) matches the code. Note: `recentTurns` drops the last turn via `slice(0, length-1)` (`yumi-brain.js:311`), so the message a reader just sent is intentionally omitted from the "Recent turns" section.
