### Findings dropped in verification (refuted)
- ~~migrate() uses ES5 Array.isArray (13√ó), which the project's ES3 cscript harness cannot evaluate ‚Äî contradicting the 'state.js is the harness-parseable file' claim~~ (state.js) ‚Äî The quantitative claims are accurate (Array.isArray = 13 hits at exactly :641,:645,:649,:1808,:1862,:1875,:1931,:1932,:1957,:1964,:2015,:2043,:2716; instanceof Array = 11√ó; const/let/arrow/template/.catch/.finally all 0 outside comments). BUT the conclusion is wrong. The harness is a PARSE-only check: .claude/parse-check-state.js does `new Function(src)` which COMPILES/PARSES the source and never EXECUTES it. `Array.isArray(...)` is syntactically valid ES3 ‚Äî an identifier `Array`, a member access `.isArray`, and a call ‚Äî so it parses cleanly; it would only fail at RUNTIME if invoked, which the harness never does. CLAUDE.md:20 explicitly calls it 'the cscript JScript PARSE harness' that 'cannot PARSE files using .catch/.finally' ‚Äî those break the PARSER (reserved-word-as-property in JScript), unlike Array.isArray which does not. state.js is genuinely parse-clean and the harness gives no false assurance about what it actually checks (parseability). The 'cannot evaluate / contradicts the harness-parseable claim' framing conflates parse with execute. False positive.


### Candidate-improvements appendix (COULD ‚Äî for the feature-proposal phase, not decisions)

### state.js saveState / sync
- **Unify the five Firestore-save blocks behind one data-driven dirty‚Üíretry‚Üípending machine** ‚Äî saveState repeats the same getCurrentUser ‚Üí typeof-guard ‚Üí buildXDoc ‚Üí saveXToFirestore ‚Üí ok/warn pattern five times (:2164-2279). Collapse to a table-driven loop over {flag, buildFn, saveFn, pendingFns} so ALL collections inherit the books-tier protection (re-dirty-on-failure + a persisted pending-sync set), eliminating the arcs/notebook/subTheories/themes data-loss asymmetry in one place and removing ~100 lines of duplication.

### state.js + UI
- **Surface a user-visible signal when a save fails (local or cloud)** ‚Äî Today both a localStorage quota failure (sv returns false, unchecked) and a cloud-write failure (console.warn) are invisible. Have saveState return a richer result and let a thin UI hook show a non-blocking 'changes not saved ‚Äî retrying' indicator, mirroring the existing 'new version ready ‚Äî Reload' banner pattern.

### state.js / account export
- **Add bookArtifacts + userThemes to exportWorkspace and a matching importWorkspace** ‚Äî Make the JSON export a complete, round-trippable backup by including the two omitted maps, and pair it with an import path (there is currently no importWorkspace anywhere ‚Äî grep returns only the export). This turns a partial export into a real disaster-recovery affordance.

### state.js clearUserState
- **Reset userThemes in clearUserState (and audit clearUserState against the default state object)** ‚Äî Drive clearUserState off the same field list as the default `state` literal (:271-285) ‚Äî e.g. iterate the known map keys ‚Äî so a newly-added top-level map can never again be forgotten by the wipe path, closing the userThemes leak structurally rather than by adding one line.

### state.js / tooling
- **Provide an ES3-safe Array.isArray shim or document state.js as harness-exempt** ‚Äî Either add a tiny `function isArr(x){return Object.prototype.toString.call(x)==='[object Array]';}` helper used uniformly (state.js already mixes Array.isArray and instanceof Array), or update CLAUDE.md to drop state.js from the cscript-parseable set so the parse gate's coverage claim is honest.

### state.js state shape
- **Retire or document the vestigial `notebooks` map** ‚Äî `state.notebooks` (:279) appears to be dead weight since schema 1.6.0 dropped notebookId (one notebook per user). Confirm no reader exists and either remove it from the default object and clear paths or annotate it as intentionally reserved.

### netlify/functions/* + js/integrations.js
- **Stop shipping the gate shared-secret in the public client bundle** ‚Äî PRAXIS_CLIENT_KEY is a static secret baked into integrations.js:18, served to every browser. It deters casual scraping but gives no real auth (trivially copyable from DevTools). If the goal is to bind proxy use to authenticated users, verify the Firebase ID token server-side in each function (the app already has Firebase Auth) instead of, or in addition to, the shared key. At minimum, treat PRAXIS_CLIENT_KEY as anti-abuse friction, not access control, and document that explicitly.

### netlify/functions/*.js (the 5 identical gate blocks)
- **Make the gate fail CLOSED in production** ‚Äî All five proxies skip the key check entirely when PRAXIS_CLIENT_KEY is unset (claude-proxy.js:23, etc.). The dev-friendly fail-open is a foot-gun: a missing/typo'd env var silently exposes the Anthropic + ElevenLabs billable endpoints to the open internet. Consider an explicit allow-anon flag (e.g. PRAXIS_ALLOW_ANON=1) so 'no key' must be a deliberate choice, with the default being reject.

### netlify/functions/*.js
- **Add a server-side request timeout to every upstream fetch in the proxies** ‚Äî None of the five functions bound their upstream fetch (Anthropic / ElevenLabs / Google Books) with an AbortController. A slow upstream can ride the full Netlify function wall-clock (10s default / 26s background) and burn invocation time. Wrap each fetch in an AbortController with a sane deadline and return a 504 the client can surface.
- **Tighten CORS from wildcard to the known origin(s)** ‚Äî Every response uses Access-Control-Allow-Origin: '*'. There is no credentialed-CORS bug (no Allow-Credentials anywhere), so this is safe today, but since the proxies are gated to one app, echoing only the praxis-reading.netlify.app origin (and localhost for dev) would reduce the blast radius if the gate is ever bypassed.

### js/yumi-brain.js (sendMessage chat path), js/integrations.js (TTS, Google Books), js/views.js (vision scan)
- **Add client-side timeouts to the user-facing proxy calls that lack them** ‚Äî _yumiWithTimeout already exists and wraps the gate/grader/web/move calls, but the primary chat fetch (yumi-brain.js:770), TTS (integrations.js:2055), Google Books (integrations.js:1447) and vision-proxy scan (views.js:5873) do not use it. The scan has a generous 20s+ ccWatchdog only on the categorize path, not on the vision fetch itself. Reuse _yumiWithTimeout (or an AbortController) so a hung upstream never leaves the chat 'thinking' forever.

### sw.js + index.html
- **Add a Cache-Control / immutable strategy and consider hashed asset URLs** ‚Äî Cache invalidation rides entirely on a manually-bumped CACHE_VERSION string; every JS change after a bump needs its own bump or the SW serves a stale bundle (called out in CLAUDE.md as a recurring hazard). Content-hashed filenames (or a build step that injects the version) would make staleness structurally impossible and remove the manual-bump discipline as a failure mode.

### js/verify-engine.js, sw.js
- **Delete or precache the verify-engine.js tombstone on a clear schedule** ‚Äî verify-engine.js (620 bytes) is a comment-only tombstone kept only to avoid a 404 during the praxis-v1 -> v2 cache rollover; its own comment says 'Safe to delete once praxis-v2 is fully adopted.' We are at praxis-v3.150. It is dead weight that is neither loaded nor precached. Remove it (and confirm no cached old client references it) to drop the file.

### netlify/functions/claude-proxy.js, vision-proxy.js
- **Cap request body size in the JSON proxies** ‚Äî transcribe-proxy enforces MAX_AUDIO_B64_CHARS (7.5M) but claude-proxy and vision-proxy JSON.parse the whole body and forward it with no size guard. vision-proxy forwards arbitrary base64 image bytes to a billable model; an oversized or malformed payload is only caught by Netlify's ~6MB platform cap. A small explicit guard returns a clean 413 and avoids a doomed upstream call.

### Yumi moves / privacy
- **Centralize the isPrivate privacy filter into one exported predicate** ‚Äî Extract isEntryVisibleToYumi(entry) and route all 7 sites (assembleContextData, artifacts, getAggregateCounts, considerMove, _visibleEntriesForScan, gatherArcContext) through it, so principle #5 has a true single enforcement point across moves too, not just chat-context.

### Yumi chat
- **Wrap sendMessage/summarizeAndRoll/generateLenses in _yumiWithTimeout** ‚Äî The timeout primitive already exists and is used by 8 other calls; applying it to the 3 untimed fetches closes the chat-lock hang and the unbounded recentTurns growth with near-zero new code.

### Yumi LLM transport
- **Add an AbortController to the timeout primitive** ‚Äî Have _yumiWithTimeout (and the wrapped fetches) pass an AbortSignal so a timeout also cancels the underlying request, preventing connection leaks under proxy degradation.

### Firestore sync
- **Add ensureArcFields/ensureThemeFields and an ensureNotebookEntryFields helper, called at each merge boundary** ‚Äî Bring arcs, themes, and notebook into the same merge-boundary backfill discipline books and sub-theories already follow, so future schema fields survive cross-device sync without per-field hand-patching.

### Yumi conversation memory
- **Persist the user turn only after a non-suppressed assistant reply (or pair them atomically)** ‚Äî Move appendTurn('user') to fire alongside appendTurn('assistant') on success, or roll back the user turn on failure/suppress, so recentTurns never carries an orphaned user line into the next buildContext.

### Yumi UI seams
- **Give maybeDrawOut and requestArcVoice explicit failure arms** ‚Äî Add a rejection handler (or .then second arg) so a future orchestrator regression that rejects cannot strand the arc-voice trigger button disabled or silently swallow a draw-out error.

### Book metadata
- **Extract categories in the lightweight fetchGoogleBooks/fetchBookByTitle paths too** ‚Äî Only volumeToBook captures rawCategories; the two lighter fetchers drop categories, so books added via those paths lack the lineage hint. Unify on volumeToBook or backfill categories there for consistent classifier coverage.

### build / bundle
- **Delete the two dead files (verify-engine.js, arcs.js) and drop them from index.html + sw.js** ‚Äî verify-engine.js is referenced nowhere; arcs.js is an empty stub. Removing both deletes 2 script tags and 1 sw precache entry, shaving a request + cache entry per client. Requires a CACHE_VERSION bump and live verify per the SW rules. Low risk (verify-engine has no loader; arcs.js only console.logs).

### views.js / arc-constellation.js / state.js / components.css
- **Remove the ~486 LOC of orphaned functions and their stranded CSS** ‚Äî openScanReviewEditor (131), _stTreatment (131), openManualLookup (79), renderArtifactCard (62), _stRenderMarks (39), _stSilhouette (35), isBookDeletePending (9), plus ~31 dead CSS rules (shelf-scan-review/manual-lookup/notebook-artifact-card). Caveat: arc-constellation.js is a declared Œî=0 invariant file ‚Äî its three dead generators may be deliberately parked; confirm with Preston before touching that file specifically.

### build harness
- **Add committed parse-check harnesses for the un-guarded ES3-clean files** ‚Äî spotlight.js, writing-canvas.js, import-capture.js (1.4k LOC), voice-input.js, and app.js all PASS ES3 parse but have no parse-check-*.js. A one-line FileSystemObject+new Function harness per file (mirroring parse-check-tfa.js) would give them the same pre-ship gate the core files have.

### Yumi
- **Introduce an ES3-safe Promise micro-shim or refactor so yumi-brain/yumi-ui regain a parse gate** ‚Äî The only thing blocking ES3 parse of the two Yumi files is .catch/.finally. Rewriting those as two-arg .then(onOk, onErr) (and a then-based finally) would let the existing cscript harness validate the frozen-gate files statically before every ship, closing the documented 'verify live only' gap. Higher-effort and touches the gate file, so gate-parity must be re-proven.
- **Thread declared values into Yumi's reader-model preamble** ‚Äî gatherReaderModel (js/yumi-brain.js:1134) could append profile.values to its return ({threads, profile, values}) under the SAME dual-consent gate (yumiReadsAlong && yumiReaderModel), and formatReaderModelPreamble (:1170) could add a 'values this reader reads toward' line with the existing anti-presumption framing. Closes the half-realized values feature without touching the frozen gate (the preamble is a pure-text prepend, like webAnglePreamble).

### rendering
- **Consolidate the three escape helpers into one shared esc()** ‚Äî Replace _arcEscapeXml, _portraitEsc, and the inline views.js escape chain with a single shared helper (decide &apos; vs &#39; once). Removes duplication and the silent divergence in entity output.

### all (substrate)
- **Add 'use strict' to views.js, state.js, arc-constellation.js, import-capture.js, writing-canvas.js, tradition-forms-arc.js** ‚Äî Brings strict mode to the largest/most-active files where accidental-global leaks are most likely. Must be live-smoke-tested per file since strict mode can surface latent sloppy-mode reliance (e.g. an undeclared assignment), but it is exactly that class of bug it would catch.

### views.js
- **Begin decomposing views.js (14,526 LOC, 53% of in-scope client)** ‚Äî The monolith is the chronic merge-contention point the build protocol already calls out. Splitting cohesive surfaces (shelf, notebook, arcs, account/portrait, artifact) into separate files behind the existing window.views export object would reduce lane collisions and make parse/CI feedback faster. Large, staged effort.

### docs
- **Reconcile CLAUDE.md's documented File load order with the actual index.html order** ‚Äî The documented order omits spotlight.js, writing-canvas.js, import-capture.js and lists arcs/integrations in a different sequence than index.html. Doc-only fix, but it is the canonical reference engineers trust for load-order reasoning.

### Global theme
- **Extend the dual-ground override to every ground-sensitive accent token** ‚Äî The override block (theme.css:336-361) covers ink/surface/gold but leaves --river, --question-color, --marginalia-color, --journal-color, --danger, --wordmark, and --gold-soft single-valued across both grounds, which is the root cause of the ¬ß3 contrast failures. The --gold-text split (muted gold-ink on bright, gold-soft on dark) is the proven pattern; apply the same per-ground brightening to the accents so each lands >=4.5:1 on the surface it is painted on. One token-only change fixes most contrast findings at once.

### Book detail / Notebook
- **Lighten --meta on bright (or add a --meta-strong for text) to clear AA** ‚Äî --meta #9a7e4e (=--ink-3/--ink-4) is the dominant meta/byline color and sits at 3.41-3.56:1 on the bright ground. Darkening it toward ~#7a6230 would clear 4.5:1 while staying within the umber family; alternatively introduce --meta-strong for the small-text uses (book-detail-meta 11px, notebook-entry-ts 10px) and reserve the lighter --meta for decorative/large use.

### Build / tooling
- **Adopt a contrast-token CI/build check** ‚Äî Since Node is blocked, a cscript JScript harness (the approved pattern) could parse theme.css token pairs and assert min contrast per ground, catching regressions like the wordmark-on-bright case before ship. Pairs are deterministic once the dual-ground resolution is encoded.

### Notebook
- **Replace stale rgba literals with their tokens to stop hue drift** ‚Äî The notebook tag borders (components.css:4123, 4129, 3236) hardcode pre-Umber teal/river hexes that no longer match the token-colored text. Swapping to color-mix(in srgb, var(--marginalia-color)/var(--question-color) ...%, transparent) keeps border and text in lockstep through future palette changes.
- **Give the user search + filter + sort over their own notes** ‚Äî A text search, a register filter (marginalia/journal/question), a date/privacy filter, and a sort would make the notebook a place you can return to your thinking. None exists today; the only structure is fixed tabs + createdAt-desc.
- **Add an optional value-tag edge on sub-theories and/or notes** ‚Äî A value-load feature wants 'this note/sub-theory advances value X'. Add a valueTags:[] field via the existing ensureBookFields/ensureSubTheoryFields chokepoint pattern (and a new ensureEntryFields chokepoint), tags drawn from profile.values. This turns the isolated values list into graph edges and enables 'show everything I've written toward <value>'.

### Global
- **Promote the remaining raw-px radii and the --scrim/black-shadow literals to tokens** ‚Äî Folding the 18 raw 10px/6px radii into --radius-md/--radius-sm, line 9989 into var(--scrim), and the three rgba(0,0,0) shadows into --shadow-* would bring components.css to a clean zero-literal state and make global radius/shadow retunes single-edit.

### global
- **Add a global reduced-motion safety-net reset** ‚Äî A single `@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce){ *,*::before,*::after { animation-duration:.01ms!important; animation-iteration-count:1!important; transition-duration:.01ms!important; scroll-behavior:auto!important } }` block would catch the ungated route-fade (components.css:5789) and any future animation, complementing the existing per-component gates rather than replacing them.
- **Establish a shared interactive-target floor** ‚Äî Add a small additive primitive (e.g. `min-height:44px; min-width:44px` or padded hit-area via ::before) for icon-only buttons and pill controls ‚Äî hamburger, .seg-opt, .nb-tab, .rm-iconbtn, .ic-close, .yumi-icon-btn ‚Äî so touch targets meet 44px without restyling each surface. The canon already calls for additive primitives (¬ß4-D).
- **Extend the :focus-visible allow-list to newer surfaces** ‚Äî The 3941-3970 allow-list predates segmented controls, notebook tabs, Yumi panel chrome, portrait toggles, and the import overlay. Append those selectors so all interactive elements share the house `outline:2px solid var(--river)` ring instead of the inconsistent UA default.
- **Re-tune --ink-3/--ink-4 (or split a light-ground meta token) for AA** ‚Äî Darken the meta value used on the bright page (a value near #6f5630 reaches ~4.5:1 on #fcf6e8) or introduce a dedicated --meta-on-light token, leaving the dark-study --muted untouched. Resolves contrast on 300+ usages of small label/eyebrow/meta text in one place.
- **Add a focus-trap helper shared by all modals** ‚Äî Only the lens panel traps focus (yumi-ui.js:1887). Factor that into a reusable trap and apply to the three views.js dialogs and the Yumi chat panel so Tab cannot escape behind an open modal.
- **Add a skip-to-content link and main landmark** ‚Äî index.html has nav then `<div id="app">` with no skip link and no role=main / <main>. A visually-hidden skip link plus a main landmark on #app would let keyboard/AT users bypass the nav on every route.

### Account / reader-portrait
- **Wire keydown bridges + tabindex on data-act delegated chips** ‚Äî The portrait dialogHost/threadsCard delegation is click-only. Add a shared keydown delegate (Enter/Space) and tabindex=0/role=button on the portrait chips and rmtoggle, mirroring the correct shelf-filter-row pattern (views.js:2986-2996) so the whole portrait flow is keyboard-operable.

### Import & capture overlay
- **Promote the import-capture overlay to a real dialog** ‚Äî Add role=dialog + aria-modal=true + aria-label, move focus into the panel on open, add a document keydown Escape-to-close, and trap Tab ‚Äî reusing the st-picker dialog pattern (views.js:6823-6825,6966) so the largest modal surface matches the others.

### Account / Import overlay
- **Confirm/establish mobile treatment for reader-portrait galaxy and import panel** ‚Äî Neither surface appears in the components.css <=759 mobile blocks; add explicit narrow-width reflow (single column, capped panel width) so they do not rely on intrinsic sizing at 390px.

### Home
- **Delete the dead Batch-4A home CSS rules and their mobile overrides** ‚Äî Remove .home-hero-title/.home-hero-accent/.home-hero-sub/.home-cta-primary/.home-cta-secondary (components.css:837-903) and their @media:759 overrides (5720-5727) once confirmed dead; collapse to the live Umber rules (961-976). ~10+ rule lines of dead weight; reduces the risk of editing ghost classes. Read-only audit found 0 JS refs.
- **Seed the demo arc with sub-theories so the Home 'living constellation' embed actually renders** ‚Äî The marquee Home preview only activates when the seed arc has sub-theories, but the migrate seed (state.js:2593-2613) creates none. Seed 2-4 inert demo sub-theories on '__praxis_seed__' so first-time visitors see the live mini-constellation the copy promises, instead of the static fallback line. Data-model touch (seed migrate), so out of a pure-CSS scope.
- **Add an explicit mobile width/cap for the home title via the live .home-title class** ‚Äî If a tighter phone title than clamp(40px,8vw,82px) is wanted (canon J implied 52px), put it on .home-title inside @media(max-width:759px) ‚Äî the current 52px rule targets dead .home-hero-title and never applies.
- **Tokenize the .home-preview shadow color** ‚Äî Replace rgba(58,40,16,.55) at components.css:914 with a shadow token (e.g. a new --shadow-brown) if the project decides to standardize shadows; aligns with the canon's no-literal-hex rule. Low value unless a broader shadow-token pass is undertaken.
- **Refresh the renderHome header comment to reflect the data-reading embed** ‚Äî Update views.js:601-602 to note that the FINALE preview reads state.seeds/arcs/subTheories, so future editors don't assume Home is state-read-free.

### Shelf
- **Wire rawCategories capture into manual + bulk-by-title add paths** ‚Äî openShelfEditor (views.js:4187) and bulk title lines (processBulkLines:4598) backfill author/isbn/cover from the resolve result but never persist volumeInfo.categories onto book.rawCategories, so manually/bulk-by-title-added books always fall through classifyBookLocal's keyword step to the LLM. Capturing the BISAC strings on the existing background fetch would let the offline keyword classifier place most of them for free, cutting LLM calls.
- **Add a per-book manual category override (the BUILD-2 hook is already stubbed)** ‚Äî views.js:3272 leaves an explicit 'preserve a manual override here once it exists: if (rb.categoryOverride) continue;' TODO in the Re-classify handler. A categoryOverride field + a book-detail picker would let users correct a misclassification durably, and Re-classify would respect it.
- **Scope Re-classify and the lazy pass to the user's shelf index** ‚Äî Re-classify (views.js:3268) iterates all of state.books; align it with the deduped shelfBookIds source the rest of renderShelf uses, so a re-classify never touches records outside the signed-in user's shelf.
- **Guard add against an existing ISBN/title before minting a new record** ‚Äî A cheap existence check in openShelfEditor / processBulkLines (match on normalized ISBN, or title+author) could offer 'already on your shelf' instead of silently creating the duplicate that Tidy library later has to merge.
- **Collapse the chip cluster into an overflow menu on mobile, or trim to canon's 3 chips** ‚Äî Either fold Scan barcode/Tidy library behind a 'More' chip at <=759, or merge the two scan entry points and demote Tidy to the Filters drawer, to bring the toolbar back to the ¬ß4-E silhouette at narrow widths.
- **Delete the ~18 stranded legacy shelf-button rules and .shelf-seg-option** ‚Äî Now that the chips use .chip, the per-button .shelf-scan-btn/.shelf-new-book-bulk/.shelf-resolve-covers-btn blocks (and the dead .shelf-seg-option) are overridden/inert; removing them shrinks components.css and removes a cascade trap.
- **Show a count or progress affordance for a long first-run classification** ‚Äî The 'Classifying N books‚Ä¶' loading row (views.js:3238) is informative, but a full library first run is a sequence of 20-book batches with no per-batch progress; surfacing batch progress (or pre-warming via rawCategories) would make the first Categories switch feel less like a stall.
- **Relate tradition/category to declared values** ‚Äî book.category (17-cat) and book.tradition (9-trad) are unrelated to profile.values. A small declared mapping (value -> traditions/categories it expresses) would let the portrait and shelf surface 'books that serve this value', the core of a value-load read.

### Arc detail (List view)
- **Render sub-theories as proper rows in the arc-detail List view** ‚Äî The header sub-meta and the Arcs-page card meta both count 'N sub-theories', but the List branch (js/views.js:9915-10002) iterates only bookIds/entryIds ‚Äî sub-theories are only reachable via the Web constellation or the dedicated subtheory page. A list of sub-theory rows (header + one-line read + maturity, linking to #subtheory/<id>) would close the count-without-a-list gap and give a non-spatial way to browse them.

### Arcs page grid
- **Migrate the arcs grid to auto-fit minmax so it is inherently responsive** ‚Äî Instead of repairing the dead id/class mismatch with another fixed-column override, '.arcs-grid { grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fit, minmax(280px, 1fr)) }' would self-collapse 3->2->1 across widths with no media query and no risk of overflow (minmax floor protects the narrow case). Removes the desktop-first base-rule fragility entirely.

### Arcs page (logged-out)
- **Give signed-out visitors a create affordance (or a sign-in nudge) on the Arcs page** ‚Äî The only create path is the dashed 'Start another arc' tile inside the user-gated Your-arcs block (js/views.js:2356-2376), so a signed-out visitor sees teaching + examples but no way to begin. A 'Sign in to build an arc' CTA under the teaching paragraph would convert the cold-start view.

### Arcs page Your-arcs grid
- **Equalize start-tile height with sibling cards instead of a fixed 300px** ‚Äî '.arcs .arc-card-start { min-height:300px }' (components.css:1830) forces the whole grid row to 300px even when the live cards are shorter, creating uneven whitespace. Letting the tile stretch to the row's natural height (align-self:stretch with a smaller min-height) would tidy the grid.

### Arcs / CSS debt
- **Remove the dead legacy arcs CSS and the orphan renderArcRow in one cleanup** ‚Äî components.css:1518-1775 (pre-Umber arcs block) and renderArcRow + its notebook-arc-row CSS (js/views.js:10925-10948; components.css:4973-5008,5361) are unreachable. Deleting them shrinks the two-generations-of-arc-card ambiguity and removes a maintenance trap where edits land on the dead block.

### Arcs page (performance)
- **Make _arcCardCounts sub-theory counting O(1)-per-arc instead of a full scan per card** ‚Äî _arcCardCounts (js/views.js:2191-2197) scans all of state.subTheories for every card rendered (O(cards x subTheories)). Building a single arcId->count map once before the render loop would make the page linear in sub-theories regardless of arc count ‚Äî cheap insurance for large libraries.

### Arc field / constellation
- **Make the constellation ground respond to dual-ground (or recolor its text to the dark-ground inks)** ‚Äî Root cause of the contrast failure: the SVG paints a fixed bright goldenrod ground (tfa-stage) while #arc went dark. Either give the sub-theory renderer a dark stage ground variant selected from data-ground, or draw the question/legend/Yumi text in tokens that stay dark-on-bright regardless of page ground (e.g. a dedicated --constellation-ink that does not remap). Pairs naturally with the dual-ground design canon.
- **Add a focus-visible ring for the live sub-theory marks** ‚Äî Add .arc-detail-web-view [data-st-sub-id]:focus-visible / [data-st-mark]:focus-visible rules mirroring the existing book-renderer ring (2px solid var(--river), offset 2px), and an outline:none reset for them. Closes the keyboard a11y gap with a few CSS lines; the JS already makes them focusable.
- **Delete the dead book-constellation renderer and its companions** ‚Äî renderArcConstellation + its ~412-LOC helper chain, _arcDetailBuildConstellationData, _arcConstellationAttachInteractions, and the matching focus-ring CSS (components.css:6222-6237) are all unreachable. Removing them shrinks the largest constellation file and removes a misleading focus-ring block. Verify nothing in spotlight/home references them first.
- **Stop emitting the 17 dead st-halo/st-grain defs** ‚Äî _stGetDefs writes a pattern + 16 gradients no live mark consumes. Trim it to only what the current recipe needs (tfa-shine is already supplied by getTraditionFormsArcDefs), or delete the call entirely after confirming. Removes 17 nodes from every render's DOM.
- **Wrap the center question label so long arc titles don't overflow** ‚Äî _stRenderQuestion (and the dead _arcRenderQuestion) render the question as a single <text> element with no wrapping; a long arc title overflows the canvas horizontally. Consider a multi-line tspan wrap at a character/width budget, mirroring the legend's two-line wrap logic.
- **Token-ize the resonance/faint edge color** ‚Äî Replace the hardcoded #966E28 on live edges (lines 1076, 1092-1094) with a --token (e.g. reuse --thread-color, which the legend already uses for the same elements) so the key and the drawn edge stay in sync and the edge participates in dual-ground remapping.
- **Remove the three superseded mark helpers** ‚Äî _stSilhouette, _stTreatment, _stRenderMarks (~200 LOC) and the unused shapeLines/_stIdentity shim are leftovers from the pre-16-mark era. A cleanup pass after confirming the 16-mark table is the sole path.

### Arc interior
- **Add ensureArcFields + array guards to close the List-render crash** ‚Äî Mirror ensureSubTheoryFields/ensureBookFields: backfill arc.bookIds/entryIds/title/description on both migrate() and the Firestore merge chokepoint, AND defensively guard the two bare reads at views.js:9924/9934 (Array.isArray). Arcs are the only top-level collection with no ensure* helper; this is the gap that crashes List view on any backfill-less arc.
- **Drop or document the dead _arcDetailBuildConstellationData** ‚Äî ~25 LOC never called (views.js:8615). If the books-constellation revert is no longer a real option, delete it; otherwise leave a dated note on why it must survive.

### Sub-theory page
- **Wire a real publish lifecycle or remove the dead status field** ‚Äî Either (a) add a publish action that sets status:'published'+publishedAt (and surface published sub-theories somewhere ‚Äî a reader view, an arc 'published theory' section), making the 'Published' toggle's name honest; or (b) delete status/publishedAt from the schema and rename the toggle to 'Preview' / 'What readers see'. Today the field implies a feature that does not exist.
- **Surface the Intellectual register in a read view (or mark it private-by-design)** ‚Äî bodyIntellectual is write-only. Decide its semantics: if it is the author's private working register, label it so and exclude it from maturity-as-public-signal; if it is meant to be read, add it to renderSubTheoryReadOnly (a second pane, or a register switch in the published view).
- **Tighten parseCitations matching to reduce false-positive citations** ‚Äî parseCitations (:7249) matches bidirectionally (span contains title OR title contains span). A short italicized word that is a substring of a long title (e.g. *the* matching a title containing 'the') resolves as a citation. Consider word-boundary or minimum-length matching, or require the span to contain the full title.

### Sub-theory linking
- **Give Unlink (and Change-mark) a non-hover home** ‚Äî Add a 'Connections' section to the sub-theory page (renderSubTheoryPage) listing linked sub-theories with a per-row Unlink, reusing confirmUnlinkSubTheory ‚Äî so touch users and List-view users can manage resonances. Today the only path is the desktop Web-view hover card. The read-only see-also list (:7448) is the natural anchor.

### Arc voice

Add a second .then arg (or .then(...).then(null, reEnable)) that renders the fallback and re-enables triggerEl. Currently latent (all links resolve) but one un-wrapped link away from a stuck affordance.

### Account / Reader-portrait
- **Make exportWorkspace the single source for 'your data' and include everything user-owned** ‚Äî Extend exportWorkspace to add uid-filtered userThemes, the readerModel (threads + arc prose + values are already in profile), and bookArtifacts, and to filter arcs/subTheories/notebookEntries by userId===uid (reuse the _accountCounts/_accountBuildCategoryPanel filtering already proven on this page). Wrapping each (or appending them before the portrait, or building all into named sub-builders guarded like the portrait sections) guarantees Export/Sign-out/Delete always render even if an upstream section throws.

- **Re-check dark-ground contrast on portrait accent copy** ‚Äî Teal/journal/danger tokens used in portrait marks and the danger affordance resolve sub-AA on the dark surface per the foundation token audit. Audit the portrait's body-adjacent meta/hint text (the gold .hint eyebrow tails, pole labels, tension sub-lines) against AA and bump to a passing token where it carries meaning rather than pure decoration.
- **Guard against renderAccountPage re-entrancy from considerProfileRefresh** ‚Äî Opening the reader-model panel can fire considerProfileRefresh which, on a successful write, calls renderAccountPage() again (js/views.js:12437-12440). Combined with the coarse re-render on every toggle/edit, the page rebuilds the entire portrait (galaxy force-sim, emblem SVG) frequently. Consider a lighter in-place update for the reader-model card, or a re-entrancy guard, to avoid rebuilding the heavy portrait on every small mutation.

### About
- **Delete the orphaned pre-Umber-port About CSS** ‚Äî Remove the ~38 dead declaration lines (about-eyebrow, about-lede-hero, about-hero-mark/-rule, hairline-gold, about-seg-wrap, about-seg-btn, and the whole rearm-card* accordion family) plus the stale first .about-seg declaration. - **Make the orientation switcher proper tabs (or proper toggle buttons)** ‚Äî Either (a) complete the tablist pattern: role=tab + aria-selected + aria-controls on the buttons, role=tabpanel + aria-labelledby on the two sections, and arrow-key roving tabindex; or (b) drop role=tablist and keep clean aria-pressed toggle-button semantics. Right now it is half of each.
- **Reconcile hero-glyph sizing to one source of truth** ‚Äî Either set data-yumi-glyph="60" to match the CSS, or drop the `.about .about-mark svg{width/height:60px}` override and let the data attribute drive size like every other crest on the page. Pick one knob.
- **Nudge normal-size secondary About text to an AA-passing ink** ‚Äî `.lex-pos` (and arguably .lex-pron) are normal-weight text at ~3.4:1 on the bright page. Consider --ink-2 for the part-of-speech/pronunciation, or accept as decorative ‚Äî but it is the one normal-size case below 4.5:1 on this surface.
- **Add a light mobile pass for the 3-col triad and wide SVG figures** ‚Äî The .triad stays 3-col at all widths (repeat(3,1fr), :9622) and the bp/ra SVGs scale to 100% of a 720->760 column; on a 390px viewport the triad cells and SVG label text get cramped. A <520px breakpoint collapsing .triad to 1-col and bumping figure label sizes would improve the narrow read. [requires live verification of actual cramping]

### Yumi panel ‚Äî chat
- **Add a timeout + AbortController to the chat reply fetch** ‚Äî Wrap sendMessage's fetch (yumi-brain.js:770) in _yumiWithTimeout (already used by all 8 other proxy calls) and/or an AbortController like import-capture.js:1054, so a stalled proxy reliably rejects into runChat's .catch ‚Üí renderError instead of hanging the typing indicator and locking Send. summarizeAndRoll (:92) and generateLenses (:926) are the other two unwrapped calls and deserve the same treatment.
- **Close the orphaned-user-turn gap on send failure** ‚Äî On a sendMessage rejection, either defer appendTurn('user') until the reply is graded/appended (append both atomically), or pop the trailing unmatched user turn in runChat's .catch so a failed send doesn't pollute memory and the transparency 'Recent turns' view. Addresses the documented 2.7b-ii-a limitation.
- **Surface a 'reaching Yumi‚Ä¶' state distinct from 'thinking' on slow networks** ‚Äî The typing indicator ('...') and Bloom 'thinking' are the only in-flight cue. If the timeout work lands, a longer-than-expected wait could swap to a soft 'still reaching Yumi‚Ä¶' line before the timeout fires, so a slow but live network reads as patience rather than a stall.

### Yumi panel ‚Äî What Yumi sees
- **Reconcile the two-ground identity of the shared transparency builder** ‚Äî buildTransparencyContent renders dark in the in-panel fold (inside .yumi-panel) and bright as the routed #yumi-sees page. Decide one canonical ground for 'What Yumi sees' (e.g. always dark to match the panel, or tag #yumi-sees dark in umberGroundDark) so the same disclosure surface has one visual identity.
- **Give #yumi-sees a logged-out sign-in prompt** ‚Äî The #yumi-sees route (views.js:581) calls renderWhatYumiSeesPage ‚Üí getContextSnapshot with no auth gate. It won't crash (resolveActiveUid returns null, loops are guarded ‚Üí empty sections), but unlike Notebook/Arcs it shows no sign-in prompt. Consider a logged-out affordance for parity. [needs live confirm of empty-state render]

### Yumi panel ‚Äî voice / CSS
- **Retire dead voice/CSS weight** ‚Äî Remove the unused VoiceInput.attachMicButton export (voice-input.js:102, ~57 LOC, zero callers) and the dead .yumi-panel-sight-link rules (components.css:241-251) flagged in-code at :10134.

### Writing
- **Adopt WritingCanvas across journal, arc-create, and artifact editors** ‚Äî Only openMarginaliaEditor uses createWritingCanvas; openJournalEditor/openArcEditor/openArtifactEditor still use the legacy raw-textarea openEditor (js/views.js:2002). Adopting the shared core would give those surfaces markdown affordances, autosave, undo, focus mode, and the same wcRenderMarkdown card rendering ‚Äî unifying the substrate. The handle contract is already substrate-agnostic; the main work is the per-surface onSave wiring (artifact needs a title field, which the canvas does not currently provide).

### Import & Capture
- **Add a client-side timeout + AbortController to segmentDoc** ‚Äî Mirror the dictation transport's TRANSCRIBE_TIMEOUT_MS pattern (js/import-capture.js:1046-1062) on segmentDoc's fetch so a slow/hung proxy degrades to renderError instead of a stuck processing beat. Pair with always passing an onType/close affordance to renderProcessing so the escape is discoverable, not just a scrim click.
- **Surface a visible close affordance on every processing beat** ‚Äî renderProcessing only adds the close button when onType is passed (:483). Always rendering a close (or a small 'Cancel' link) would make the bulk-import 'Reading your notes‚Ä¶' beat escapable without relying on the undiscoverable scrim click on ov.
- **Guard large uploads with a size cap + chunked or paged segmentation** ‚Äî Add a byte/char threshold before segmentDoc; over it, either warn the user or split the document into multiple <=budget segmentation calls so no note is silently dropped under max_tokens:4096 (js/import-capture.js:137,462).

### Spotlight (‚åòK)
- **Filter/deep-link spotlight author and note results** ‚Äî Route author rows to a shelf filtered by that author and note rows to the notebook scrolled/highlighted to the entry, instead of the generic #books/#notebook (js/spotlight.js:134,176). Would make those two groups deliver on the specificity their labels imply.
- **Token-source the spotlight idea-chip inner-light color** ‚Äî Replace the literal #FFF8E7 (js/spotlight.js:240) with a CSS var (e.g. a --chip-core / --tfa-innerL token) read at build time, so the chip core and constellation mark core never drift.
- **Make Spotlight note results actually navigate to the note** ‚Äî Route a note hit to its owning tab and scroll/flash the entry (carry the entry id + tabKey through spotlight.js:173-177 and have renderNotebook honour a target). Right now search finds notes it cannot take you back to.

### Writing (marginalia)
- **Provide an explicit delete/clear path from the marginalia canvas** ‚Äî Because flushSave never persists empty (js/writing-canvas.js:526), an emptied note keeps a stale body. A 'Delete note' affordance on the Done bar (calling deleteEntry on the session's entryId) would let a reader actually remove a marginalia note from the editor instead of leaving an orphan.

### subtheory
- **Adopt the shared WritingCanvas (live-markdown) for the sub-theory register bodies** ‚Äî The marginalia editor already routes through createWritingCanvas (views.js:10156, shipped v3.150). The sub-theory page is the lone holdout on the older split-pane Write\|Preview textarea model (views.js:7582-7596). Unifying on WritingCanvas would give inline rendering as-you-type, autogrow, and one writing substrate across the app ‚Äî the single biggest lever toward an Apple/Claude-grade composer. The cite-weave layer would need to live on top of (or be folded into) the canvas's render path.
- **Implement a real publish/register transition (finish ‚Üí public)** ‚Äî The schema is already there (status, publishedAt ‚Äî state.js:660-671) and the published read-only render is built (renderSubTheoryReadOnly mode 'published', views.js:7285). Wire a state mutator (setSubTheoryStatus) + a real 'Publish'/'Finish' action that stamps status='published'/publishedAt, then surface published sub-theories somewhere readers can find them. This closes the named flow's missing terminal step.
- **Bring Yumi into the sub-theory margin** ‚Äî Add a solicited (or budgeted gated) draw-out/complicate slot on the writing page mirroring the arc-voice pattern (considerArcVoice, views.js:9379) and the notebook's resting COMPLICATE placeholder (views.js:1189). The author arguing a claim from cited evidence is exactly where a 'complicate, never a verdict' question lands hardest.
- **Add keyboard affordances to the composer** ‚Äî No metaKey/ctrlKey handlers exist on the page (grep empty). A ‚åò‚Üµ / ‚åòK to cite the last-focused evidence, ‚åòP to toggle Preview, and ‚åòS as an explicit flush would make the surface keyboard-first and harden the blur-only save path.
- **Word-boundary / exact-title citation matching** ‚Äî Replace the bidirectional substring match (views.js:7249) with an exact or word-boundary-anchored match (optionally longest-title-wins) so short/common titles don't spuriously resolve or trigger false ambiguity.
- **Autosave prose on debounced input + flush on route change** ‚Äî Add a debounced input-save (reuse the existing 200ms cite debounce shape, views.js:8082) and an activeElement.blur()/flush in renderRoute before host.innerHTML='' so in-flight prose can never be lost to a hash navigation. Pairs naturally with the WritingCanvas adoption.
- **Confirm-or-defer empty-draft creation from the arc page** ‚Äî The arc '+ Sub-theory' click mints an empty untitled draft immediately (views.js:483) with no title prompt, leaving stray drafts on accidental clicks. Either open an inline name field first (like the notebook gather flow) or mark unsaved-empty drafts for auto-cleanup.
- **Make maturity qualitative, not just length¬∑evidence arithmetic** ‚Äî _stComputeMaturity (views.js:8754) is purely (chars + 80¬∑evidenceCount)/1500. Consider factoring in citation density (cited vs uncited evidence), register coverage (both Public and Intellectual present), and linked sub-theories so the band reflects argument quality, not keystroke volume ‚Äî or relabel it honestly as a 'fullness' indicator.

### Arcs list (#arcs)
- **Navigate to the new arc's detail (or scroll to its card) after create** ‚Äî openArcEditor save calls renderRoute() which just re-paints #arcs; the new arc appears somewhere in the 3-up grid with no acknowledgement. createArc returns the arc record (js/views.js:2152) so location.hash='#arc/'+arc.id would land the user inside the thing they just made ‚Äî stronger feedback loop, and it teaches the interior immediately.
- **Unify the two .arc-card CSS systems and delete the cover-thumbnail rules** ‚Äî Fold the pre-Umber .arc-card block (components.css 1610-1808) into the .arcs .arc-card block: drop the leaking padding:20px, remove dead .arc-card-text/.arc-card-description/.arc-card-covers/.arc-card-cover*/duplicate .arc-card-meta. One card system reduces the cascade-surprise risk on this surface.

### Arc interior ‚Äî Web view
- **Give book squares a hover tooltip and keyboard focus in the Web view** ‚Äî Mirror the sub-theory treatment: bind a title/author tooltip and _arcMakeFocusable over bookSquareEls (js/views.js:8989). Resolves the keyboard-blocker and lets a reader identify a book before clicking. The data is already on arc.bookIds ‚Üí state.books.
- **Label books in the field, or thumbnail them, instead of anonymous squares** ‚Äî _stRenderBooks draws featureless --sunk squares (arc-constellation.js:1212). A tiny spine-chip or first-letters glyph (the rail already builds a .mc spine chip with the title) would let books read as identifiable members of the field rather than placeholder marks the legend has to explain.

### Arc interior ‚Äî Web view, mobile
- **Add a tap-to-preview affordance for touch in the constellation** ‚Äî Because all hover paths are !isTouch-gated, touch users get no preview. A first-tap-shows-card / second-tap-navigates pattern (or a persistent bottom info strip reflecting the last-tapped mark) would restore identity on phones without a hover dependency.

### Arc constellation + interior
- **Remove the dead book-era constellation substrate** ‚Äî renderArcConstellation + 9 helpers (~409 LOC, arc-constellation.js 59-467), the _arcConstellation* interaction cluster (~290 LOC, views.js 9033-9322), _arcDetailBuildConstellationData (8615), renderArcRow (10925), and _stTreatment/_stRenderMarks/_stSilhouette. ~750+ LOC of confirmed-dead arc code; the source itself flags the _st* trio for 'later cleanup'.

### Arc interior navigation
- **Reconcile the Arcs‚ÜîNotebook surface model so exits return where the user came from** ‚Äî Either route interior exits (not-found, delete, stale-note) back to #arcs (where Your-arcs cards live) or reinstate an arc list on #notebook. Today the delete-redirect comment asserts a Notebook arc list that no longer exists. Track from-route to return the user to their entry surface.

### Arcs list + interior
- **Share one count helper between the list card and the interior sub-meta** ‚Äî _arcCardCounts (views.js:2185) and the inline interior sub-meta loop (9562-9585) independently re-walk state.subTheories per arc. A single counts helper removes the duplication and guarantees the card meta and the interior header can never disagree.

### Notebook spread / Book detail
- **Add an inline note-detail / read-more so a clipped note can be read in full** ‚Äî Either remove the overflow:hidden clip (components.css:10615) in favour of a 'Read full note' expander, or add a lightweight #entry/<id> reading view. Today a long marginalia note's tail is unreachable; the focus area is precisely re-reading one's own thinking.

### renderNotebookEntry
- **Render markdown for ALL registers (or for none) so displayed writing matches composed writing** ‚Äî Drop the `isMarg &&` guard at js/views.js:10705 and route every register through wcRenderMarkdown, or standardise on plain text everywhere. The capture surface (plain textarea, all registers) and import paths already accept markdown into journal/question.

### Account reader-portrait
- **Surface real note text in the reader-portrait, linked from the counts** ‚Äî RETURNS/GALAXY/THREADS show only counts and shapes (js/views.js:12945+). Let 'Book X ‚Äî 7 notes' expand to or link to those 7 notes, so the portrait connects the aggregate back to the actual writing it summarises.

### Account page
- **Collapse the duplicated reader-model threads + double consent toggle into one block** ‚Äî Remove the portrait-threads duplicate listing (js/views.js:13826) or the buildReaderModelSection threads list (js/views.js:12304) so themes and the yumiReaderModel switch appear exactly once per page.

### renderNotebookEntry body
- **Switch note body from full-italic 20px serif to an upright reading style; reserve italic for emphasis** ‚Äî Adopt the upright .notebook-entry-body-md treatment (or --font-body) as the base body style for long-form legibility, matching the design canon's font-role split.

### Notebook pickers / transparency
- **Convert the inline picker/transparency panels into real overlays with focus + scroll-into-view** ‚Äî openTransparencyView, openEntryArcPicker, openEntrySendToSubTheory, openFileToBookPicker mount inline with no backdrop/focus-trap/scroll target, so on a long card they open below the fold and read as inert blocks. A consistent overlay primitive (it exists for the spotlight modal) would fix this.

### Notebook right leaf
- **Replace the inert COMPLICATE / name-block placeholders in the right leaf with real affordances or reclaim the space** ‚Äî The hardcoded 'Once Yumi's reading along, she'll open a question here' block (js/views.js:1189-1208) occupies prime composing space doing nothing; either wire it or remove it until it ships.

### renderNotebookEntry source line
- **Show full marginalia source for multi-book notes** ‚Äî Render all attributed book titles (or 'from X +N more') instead of only bookIds[0] (js/views.js:10692), so cross-book marginalia keeps the associations the reader assigned.

### sub-theory compose
- **Adopt WritingCanvas for the sub-theory public/intellectual registers** ‚Äî Replace the two raw subtheory-register-body textareas (views.js:7582/7590) with two WritingCanvas instances, giving the platform's main long-form surface autogrow, live markdown, toolbar and autosave-cue. Requires reconciling parseCitations (citation numbering + private-evidence exclusion) with wcRenderMarkdown ‚Äî likely a citation-aware display renderer layered on the shared markdown renderer so editor and published view finally match.

### notebook / book detail
- **Unify the two marginalia doors** ‚Äî Make the notebook writeline and openMarginaliaEditor share one substrate so marginalia is composed identically wherever it is entered. Either promote the writeline to a compact WritingCanvas, or downgrade the book-detail editor to match ‚Äî but pick one so a register is never authored two ways.

### journal / artifact / arc editors
- **Route journal / artifact / arc-create bodies through the shared core** ‚Äî openEditor's fixed-rows textarea backs three surfaces (journal, artifact, arc description). Swapping it for the WritingCanvas (or at least JS autogrow + the shared markdown display) would give them growth and consistent formatting with one change, since they already funnel through one helper.

### all textarea surfaces
- **Give every prose textarea autogrow as a minimum baseline** ‚Äî Short of full WritingCanvas adoption, extract the writeline's autogrowWriteline (views.js:1539) into a shared utility and apply it to the evidence, reader-model, arc-profile and openEditor bodies so no prose field requires manual resize-drag.

### writing-canvas core
- **Add a flushSave() to destroy() and a route-teardown for the canvas** ‚Äî Have destroy() flush the pending save before clearing the timer, and register a teardown on route change so navigating away saves and clears the wc-focus nav-dim even when blur does not fire. Hardens durability and prevents a leaked dimmed nav.
- **Author and commit design/writing-core-contract.md** ‚Äî Write the substrate-agnostic handle contract the header already references, as the authoritative spec future adopters bind to ‚Äî the core was explicitly designed for multi-surface adoption, so the contract should be a real, versioned file.

### notebook cards
- **Extend wcRenderMarkdown to journal/question cards** ‚Äî Marginalia cards render markdown via wcRenderMarkdown (views.js:10707) but journal/question cards fall back to plain textContent (10709). If markdown is a first-class authoring feature, the non-marginalia cards should render it too for a consistent reading surface.

### Arcs
- **Build a stored reverse index from book/note -> citing sub-theories** ‚Äî Every reverse lineage traversal today is an O(all-sub-theories x evidence) full scan (e.g. the delete cascade at js/views.js:5473-5485). A maintained reverse index (refId -> [subTheoryId]) updated in addEvidence/deleteSubTheory would make 'what did this book contribute to' cheap and is a prerequisite for a lineage view.

### Account
- **Give arcs and themes a field chokepoint + export coverage** ‚Äî Add ensureArcFields/ensureThemeFields/ensureEntryFields mirroring ensureBookFields, call them in the Firestore merge (js/integrations.js arc/theme/notebook branches), and add userThemes+bookArtifacts to exportWorkspace. Makes the whole value/lineage substrate future-proof for new fields and fully portable.
- **Surface evidence quote+annotation as a lineage trail in the portrait** ‚Äî Evidence already carries {quote, annotation, refId} (js/state.js:2018-2026) ‚Äî a true lineage edge with the supporting passage. The portrait emblem (js/views.js:13005) draws counts only; it could render the actual value->arc->sub-theory->quoted-source path so the reader sees the lineage, not just an abstract emblem.


## Open questions for the design phase

- **Durability model for non-book records.** Books alone re-dirty on cloud-save failure and carry a persisted `pendingBookSync` guard; arcs/notebook/subTheories/themes have neither and can be lost under REPLACE-on-auth. Do we extend the books pattern to all five maps, or rethink the REPLACE-on-auth merge into a non-destructive reconcile? This is the audit's top finding and needs a product call on the durability guarantee we make to writers.

- **Artifact + lens + reader-model persistence and export scope.** Artifacts are localStorage-only; `exportWorkspace` omits `bookArtifacts`, `userThemes` (lenses), and the reader-model, and leaks unfiltered seed/cross-user arcs/subTheories/notebookEntries. Decide what "take a copy of your data" must include and whether Artifacts/lenses are cloud-synced first-class objects or local conveniences.

- **Sub-theory publish lifecycle.** `status`/`publishedAt` exist in the schema but no path ever sets `published` and nothing reads it ‚Äî there is no terminal public state for the central artifact. Is "publish" an in-scope 2.0 feature (with a public read surface), or should the inert field and "Published" preview-only button be removed as implied-but-absent debt?

- **Intellectual register visibility.** The second register the UI invites authors to fill (`bodyIntellectual`) is never surfaced in any read or published view. Is it author-only scaffolding by design, or should the published/read render expose both registers?

- **Writing-core unification.** `createWritingCanvas` (live markdown, toolbar, autosave, undo, focus mode) is adopted at only 1 of 8+ prose surfaces; the notebook writeline, sub-theory registers, journal/question notes, and the Artifact editor are divergent raw textareas where only marginalia renders markdown. Decide the canonical writing substrate and the migration order ‚Äî this is the central 2.0 unification debt.

- **Markdown rendering consistency across registers.** Only marginalia routes through `wcRenderMarkdown`; journal and question notes show raw `#`/`**` back to their authors, and sub-theory bodies render via a citation-only parser that leaves `**bold**` literal. Is markdown a platform-wide contract for all composed text, or marginalia-only?

- **Mobile constellation experience.** Every hover/preview/unlink affordance is gated on `!isTouch`, book squares are keyboard-unreachable and unlabeled, and the feeding arc-card grid stays 3-up at 390px ‚Äî so the Web view is effectively unusable on phones, the primary surface this audit targets. Decide the mobile interaction model (tap-to-preview vs tap-to-navigate, touch unlink path).

- **Constellation Layers / legend rebuild scope.** Design-spec C.3/C.4 (Layers as toggle switches, 5-item legend, slow drift, "the question" center label, book-evidence layer) remain the canonical future target but are explicitly deferred; meanwhile ~600+ LOC of dead book-constellation renderer and helpers are carried in load-bearing files. Decide whether this build restyles-only or commits to the Layers rebuild ‚Äî and whether to delete the dead renderer now.

- **Categories Stage 2 scope.** `volumeToBook` now captures `rawCategories` and an LLM classifier exists, but re-classify wipes `book.category` across all of `state.books` (not the user's shelf set) and the shelf toolbar still ships 5 chips vs canon's 3. Define the classify trigger, the taxonomy authority, and the decluttered toolbar shape.

- **Lineage / value model.** `profile.values` (the portrait "stones") are stored and drawn but never reach Yumi's reader-model context (`gatherReaderModel`/`assembleContextData` have no values slot), `userThemes` lack an export/backfill chokepoint, and the reader-model threads + consent toggle render twice on the Account page behind one bit. Decide whether declared values steer Yumi and how the lineage substrate (values, lenses, threads) is unified, exported, and consented.

- **Accessibility contrast pass strategy.** A large share of secondary text (the `--meta` ink used 300+ times, plus river/teal/journal/danger/wordmark) is sub-AA on at least one ground because single-valued tokens are not remapped per ground. Decide whether to add per-ground variants for these accent tokens or darken the base values ‚Äî and set the WCAG target (AA vs AAA) for the redesign.

- **Modal / keyboard accessibility baseline.** Multiple interactive controls advertise `role=button`/`role=tablist` but are keyboard-dead or mis-wired (portrait toggle, offer chips, About tabs), dialogs and the Yumi panel don't trap focus, and touch targets run 26-36px. Decide the a11y conformance bar for 2.0 and whether a shared focus-trap/keyboard-bridge primitive is in scope.

---

## Requires live verification

_Claims that could not be confirmed statically ‚Äî for Claude-in-Chrome or Preston to check on praxis-reading.netlify.app._

- [ ] (state.js) On a device under a transient Firestore failure, create or edit an arc (or a journal entry, sub-theory, or theme), confirm the console shows 'saveArcsToFirestore: failed', then sign in on a second device and verify whether the arc/entry/sub-theory/theme is LOST after the REPLACE-on-auth merge (this is the CRITICAL data-loss path; books should survive the same test via pendingBookSync).
- [ ] (state.js) In a browser with localStorage quota exhausted or in private/incognito mode where setItem throws, perform any save action and confirm whether the app gives ANY user-visible or console signal that the save failed (expected today: none ‚Äî saveState returns false unchecked).
- [ ] (state.js) Sign in as user A on a shared browser, create a manual theme, sign out, sign in as user B, and inspect state.userThemes in the console BEFORE any Firestore load completes to confirm user A's themes are still present in memory (clearUserState omits userThemes).
- [ ] (state.js) Click the account 'Export to JSON' button and inspect the downloaded file to confirm bookArtifacts and userThemes are absent from the exported object.
- [ ] (state.js) Confirm whether the cscript JScript ES3 harness actually parses/executes js/state.js end-to-end given the 13 Array.isArray uses, or whether it errors/skips on them (CLAUDE.md claims state.js is the harness-validatable file).
- [ ] (proxies + sw) [requires live verification] With PRAXIS_CLIENT_KEY set in Netlify, POST to /.netlify/functions/claude-proxy with a wrong/absent x-praxis-key returns 401 {"error":"unauthorized"} (and the same for elevenlabs-proxy, google-books-proxy, transcribe-proxy, vision-proxy). Confirm via curl against praxis-reading.netlify.app.
- [ ] (proxies + sw) [requires live verification] Confirm PRAXIS_CLIENT_KEY is actually SET in the live Netlify environment (memory notes the SEC gate header was 'INERT until Preston sets the Netlify env var'). If unset, all 5 proxies are fully open to any caller. Test: POST with NO x-praxis-key header; a 200 (not 401) proves the gate is currently fail-open in production.
- [ ] (proxies + sw) [requires live verification] Trigger an upstream hang (or a very slow Anthropic response) and confirm the main Yumi chat (yumi-brain.js sendMessage, fetch at yumi-brain.js:770) either resolves or shows an error within a bounded time. Static read shows this fetch has NO AbortController/timeout, so it may hang indefinitely on the user-facing chat surface.
- [ ] (proxies + sw) [requires live verification] On a hard refresh after a CACHE_VERSION bump, confirm the update banner ('A new version of Praxis is ready') appears and Reload promotes the waiting SW (SKIP_WAITING -> controllerchange -> reload). The fetch handler deliberately skips respondWith on API/streaming URLs to avoid pinning the active worker.
- [ ] (proxies + sw) [requires live verification] Confirm /js/verify-engine.js is never requested by any live client (it is in neither index.html nor the sw.js precache). If some cached old client still references it, confirm it 404s gracefully without breaking load.
- [ ] (yumi + integrations) [requires live verification] Confirm that a hung claude-proxy connection (simulate via DevTools network throttle/offline mid-request) leaves the Yumi chat send button permanently disabled with the typing indicator stuck, recoverable only by reload ‚Äî proving the sendMessage no-timeout HIGH finding end-to-end.
- [ ] (yumi + integrations) [requires live verification] On the live deploy, run window.YumiGateHarness(), window.YumiMoveHarness(), window.YumiArcVoiceHarness(), and window.YumiRouterHarness() and confirm the gate is 10/10, the router covenant failures == 0, and the move harness shows no 'DRIFT-SUPPRESS' rows.
- [ ] (yumi + integrations) [requires live verification] Sign in on a second device whose remote /userArcs or /userThemes doc predates a (hypothetical) new per-record field and confirm whether arcs/themes render correctly without the field ‚Äî characterizing the real-world impact of the no-backfill arc/theme merge.
- [ ] (yumi + integrations) [requires live verification] Send a chat message that the gate suppresses (or force a proxy failure), then send a second message, and inspect state.users[uid].yumiMemory.recentTurns / 'what Yumi sees' to confirm the orphaned user turn from sendMessage persists into the next context.
- [ ] (yumi + integrations) [requires live verification] Add a book via the ISBN/title resolveBook path and confirm book.rawCategories is populated from Google Books volumeInfo.categories, then confirm the Stage-2 classifier assigns a category ‚Äî verifying the categories-capture path is live, not just present in source.
- [ ] (yumi + integrations) [requires live verification] Confirm the cscript JScript parse harness cannot parse yumi-brain.js / yumi-ui.js (due to .catch/.finally) and that these files are therefore only ever validated on the live deploy, per the CLAUDE.md note.
- [ ] (ES3 + dead weight) [requires live verification] Confirm that removing js/arcs.js and js/verify-engine.js (and their index.html script tags + the sw.js precache entry for arcs.js) does not 404 or break startup on a hard-refreshed client after a CACHE_VERSION bump ‚Äî older cached clients should still load.
- [ ] (ES3 + dead weight) [requires live verification] Confirm the dead-function removals (openScanReviewEditor, openManualLookup, renderArtifactCard, _stTreatment/_stRenderMarks/_stSilhouette, isBookDeletePending) are truly unreachable at runtime ‚Äî drive the Shelf scan/add flows, the Notebook artifact stream, and the Arcs constellation render to verify no path invokes them via an event handler the static grep could not see.
- [ ] (ES3 + dead weight) [requires live verification] Confirm adding 'use strict' to views.js/state.js/etc. does not surface a latent sloppy-mode dependency (e.g. an undeclared global assignment) that throws at runtime ‚Äî smoke every core surface (Home, Shelf, Arcs list+web, Notebook, Account/portrait, Yumi) with a clean console after the change.
- [ ] (ES3 + dead weight) [requires live verification] Since yumi-brain.js and yumi-ui.js cannot be ES3 parse-validated by the harness, any edit to them must be syntax-verified on the live deploy (chat round-trip + clean console) rather than via cscript.
- [ ] (tokens + contrast) [requires live verification] On the bright Notebook page, confirm the 'Add to an arc' link (.notebook-entry-add-to-arc, --wordmark/#e7c46a on cream) is the computed ~1.5:1 pale-gold-on-cream and visually near-illegible; use DevTools getComputedStyle to read the resolved color against the surface.
- [ ] (tokens + contrast) [requires live verification] On a dark-ground surface with the Yumi panel open, confirm the .ground-chip.web (river) and .ground-chip.theme (teal) label text resolve to #3a5a8a/#2e8a93 over --surface-d (1.98:1 / 3.41:1) - the dark override does not remap --river/--marginalia-color, so confirm the chips read low-contrast in the live DOM.
- [ ] (tokens + contrast) [requires live verification] On the bright Book-detail page, verify .book-detail-meta (11px --ink-3) and on Notebook .notebook-entry-ts (10px --ink-4) resolve to --meta #9a7e4e (3.41-3.56:1), confirming --ink-3/--ink-4 take the bright value on these routes (not the dark --muted).
- [ ] (tokens + contrast) [requires live verification] Confirm js/views.js:369 ground mapping at runtime: that #book, #subtheory, #notebook, #about render with body[data-ground=bright] and #home/#books/#arcs/#arc/#account render data-ground=dark, so the contrast pairs above are evaluated against the correct resolved surface per route.
- [ ] (tokens + contrast) [requires live verification] Verify the --grad primary-button text (--br-deep on the 92deg #d2a23e->#2e8a93 gradient) stays >=4.5:1 across the gradient midpoint, not just the endpoints (7.88:1 start, 4.54:1 end computed); the mid-gradient sample needs a live eyedropper check.
- [ ] (a11y + responsive) At 390px device-mode, verify the reader-portrait galaxy/axis section and the import-capture .ic-panel reflow to a single column without horizontal overflow or clipped controls (no components.css <=759 block was found for these surfaces).
- [ ] (a11y + responsive) With the keyboard only, open Account > reader portrait, Tab to the 'Let Yumi notice' toggle and press Enter/Space ‚Äî confirm it does NOT toggle (predicted keyboard-dead; handler at views.js:13857 is click-only).
- [ ] (a11y + responsive) With the keyboard only, on a Yumi-named lens offer in the portrait dialog, attempt to Tab to and activate the confirm/rename/reject chips ‚Äî confirm they cannot be reached or activated (predicted: click-only spans, no tabindex).
